Current Affairs Commentary

Re-Discussion on France Occupying Nine Small Islands in China's South Sea 14

From April 7th to 12th of this year, the French navy planted the tricolor flag on nine small islands in China's South Sea. On July 14th, this matter was slightly leaked. By the 25th, they announced the official occupation. The nine islands are: Cayeux, Damas, Paize, Ituba, Deux, Laitou, Titu, Spratly Island, and two attached islands. They are located between French Annam, British Borneo, and American Philippines, about one hundred and several tens of *li* from the Guangdong coast. The total area of the nine islands is three hundred *mu*, less than half a square mile. Since the French announcement, all sectors of China have been greatly shocked. Although only fishermen have resided on these islands in the past, the right of territorial ownership cannot be infringed upon. Now, French warships have suddenly announced their occupation, which is no different from aggression. Moreover, at the same time, the Japanese side is widely spreading the news that the islands were discovered long ago by Japanese merchants, expressing their determination to compete with the French. International disputes seem to be just beginning and not yet over. The French initially did not want this matter to attract international attention, saying that the occupation of the nine islands was only for navigational convenience. Later, in view of the reactions from various parties, they argued that it was an "occupation without any imperialistic implications." However, in any case, the issue of the occupation of these small islands has aroused close international attention.

We should observe this issue from two perspectives: our national sovereignty and international relations. First, from the aspect of our national sovereignty, the nine islands occupied by the French are indeed our territory. Therefore, the government should make a resolute protest to the French. Upon investigating the location of the nine islands announced by the French, they are said to be located at 10 degrees north latitude and 115 degrees east longitude, seemingly close to our Xisha Islands, or perhaps part of the archipelago. The French have long coveted the Xisha Islands. Three years ago, they even made an attempt to occupy them. The dispute of that day remains an outstanding issue. There are more than twenty islands, large and small, in the Xisha Islands, scattered in the sea. Those being occupied this time may just be the small islands at the southern end. Yesterday, a Havas Paris dispatch reported that the French government occupied Spratly Island, the largest of the nine islands, on April 13, 1930, which is possible evidence. Although coastal islands may be of no economic value, they play an important role in defending the border. In the past century, China has been left wide open due to the occupation of coastal islands. Now, these islands are again coveted by a strong neighbor. Whether for the sake of sovereignty or border defense, the Chinese government cannot but argue with reason. Second, from the perspective of international relations, the French occupation of the nine small islands is nothing less than a prelude to the great powers returning to the policy of striving for and safeguarding colonies. The claim of navigational convenience is a clear pretext, while the military purpose is an undeniable fact. The nine islands are located halfway between Singapore and Hong Kong, shielding Annam. In terms of France's position in the Far East, their military effectiveness is significant. From another perspective, what benefits France inevitably harms other countries. Therefore, after the French occupation, the Tokyo telegraph broadcast the atmosphere that the Japanese had previously occupied them. There are two versions of the story. One is that a Japanese merchant named Hashimoto requested the Japanese government to occupy the islands on October 7, 1918. Another is that a man named Hirata Suetsugu operated a mine on the island and named the islands the Hirata Islands. The fierce competition between Japan and France over these nine small islands is already evident. Remembering the beginning of the September 18th Incident, Britain and France, with a compromising attitude, hoped that the Japanese would be the protectors of the colonies of the great powers in the Far East. When Japan broke away from the League of Nations and its ambition for exclusive control was exposed, the imperialists realized the need to protect their colonies with their own strength. The failure of the London Economic Conference further promoted this trend. However, the promotion of this trend, whether in tangible or intangible ways, seems to be aimed at China's borders. The Hengqin Island case has not long passed, and the nine islands in the South Sea have been invaded and occupied again. Looking to the future, it is chilling.

It has been five or six days since the French government announced the occupation of the nine islands, and the Chinese government is still in the midst of "dispatching personnel for surveying" and "preparing protests." Diplomatic actions should be practical and swift. The geographical situation of the nine islands should be carefully investigated. However, completing the investigation in the shortest possible time and lodging a serious protest is the common demand of the people. If we procrastinate and act perfunctorily, the greed of the strong will be unlimited. Are the future troubles of our country still imaginable?

Trade Pressure on Japan from Various Countries 15

Japan Plans Fundamental Countermeasures (Tokyo) Since the adjournment of the Economic Conference, the pressure from Britain on trade with Japan has become increasingly apparent. Australia and the Malay Federation are also gradually discussing raising tariffs, and the Union of South Africa also advocates trade pressure on Japan, which makes Japan's future foreign trade situation even more significant. Therefore, the foreign affairs authorities are also studying permanent countermeasures, and have now established the following fundamental guidelines, which will soon be proposed to the relevant authorities and private sector operators, in order to promote the development of Japan's trade organization: (1) Domestic countermeasures: Use the Trade Council to establish an organized trade policy, while urging private exporters to carry out voluntary export controls. If voluntary control is difficult, establish an export association law to control exports with the power of the government. Also, in overseas markets, prohibit the auctioning and unfair dumping of exporters by means of laws. (2) Foreign countermeasures: Revise the past liberalism and unconditional most-favored-nation treatment treaty, and base it on the principle of individual reciprocal negotiation. The establishment of a trade agreement with a foreign country must be agreed to, but the agreement is limited to quantity agreements, excluding market agreements and price agreements. Also, take the agreement as a principle, and use it as an agreement between the other country and Japanese operators. In addition, adapt to the trade relations between the other country and Japan. Furthermore, between the government and operators of the other country, set a certain commodity and a certain amount of barter agreement. (30th day, Dentsu telegraph)

(Tokyo) After the adjournment of the Economic Conference, the main points of the financial and economic policies of the Japanese Ministry of Finance are as follows: (1) Compile the next year's budget. Due to the breakdown of the economic meeting and the confrontation between countries, the tendency of joint economy has further promoted the construction of the economic union between Japan and Manchuria, and the budget expanded due to this is unavoidable. The financial resources of the budget are in the process of restoring the economy. At present, it is difficult to increase taxes and expand official industries. It is necessary to seek public achievements. (2) Trade policy: In accordance with commercial ethics and the export control of the association, ensure the existing market, and must move towards opening up new markets. (3) Tariff policy: If a foreign country starts an unreasonable tariff war, Japan will also carry out retaliatory tariffs. When necessary, grant the Minister of Finance or the Minister of Commerce and Industry the autocratic power of the tariff law. (4) Exchange rate policy: The exchange rate for speculation, etc., is fully controlled by the application of the exchange rate management law. As for the exchange rate balance setting fund system, it is not only difficult to implement, but also considered unnecessary. Therefore, with the goal of enriching the economic and financial situation without deteriorating the domestic finances and without changing the exchange rate, we will quietly observe the market activity. (5) Low-interest policy: Thorough low-interest policy, and strive to restore and promote the economy. (30th day, Dentsu telegraph)

The Future of Japan's Kwantung Army After Mutō's Death 16

(Tokyo) Internal disputes within the Kwantung Army have been intensifying since the time of General Mutō. The conflict between Mutō and Koiso has been rumored among the Japanese that General Mutō's actions have lost their freedom. Some say that Lieutenant General Koiso will be transferred to be the commander of his division during the regular move in August. The rumors are inconsistent. Originally, Lieutenant General Koiso was not from the Araki faction. Although he was close to Ugaki, he was not from the Ugaki faction. He was a fighter from the middle faction. His intelligence and ability to handle things well have allowed him to reach his current position. After Mutō's death, Koiso has lost his opponent, and the new commander is also from the middle faction, so the internal disputes within the Kwantung Army may disappear from now on. However, there are many members of the Araki faction in the Kwantung Army. The dispute between the commander and the chief of staff may be eliminated, but the opposition between the two factions is not easy to resolve, or it may lead to further internal strife from now on. The future is still difficult to predict. (30th day, China United Press)

Japan's Shipping Industry in Our Country Suffers a Crushing Defeat 19

Ministry of Communications Increases Subsidies by 2 Million Yen Compared to Last Year (Tokyo) The expiration date of the Ministry of Communications' mandated routes will be from March to December of next year. Due to the depression in the shipping industry, various shipping companies have requested an increase in route subsidies. The Ministry of Communications, in view of the importance of the routes to the United States and China, decided to increase the subsidy for the North American route by 950,000 yen, and the coastal and Yangtze River routes in China by 770,000 yen. Therefore, the total amount of route subsidies in the 9th fiscal year budget reached 21,339,000 yen, an increase of 1,939,000 yen compared to last year. (30th day, Dentsu telegraph)

Page 8

500,000 Unemployed Have Jobs After Roosevelt's Recovery Plan is Implemented 20

Working Hours Reduced to 35 Hours Per Week, Lowest Wages Average About 14 Yuan Per Week, Capitalists Have Slight Objections to This Plan (New York) An investigation into the national situation in the United States shows that after the implementation of the National Industrial Recovery Act next Monday, at least 500,000 unemployed people will be able to get jobs on Monday morning. Their lowest wages will average 14 yuan per week, and the earnings of skilled workers will be far more than this. It is estimated that the wages of these newly employed people will be close to 10 million yuan per week, which will be of great benefit to the people's livelihood. As for child labor, it is expected to be abolished in about ten days, because it is extremely uneconomical to hire child labor under the new minimum wage regulations. As for working hours, they are reduced to an average of 35 hours per week. However, many large industries plan to keep machines running for 80 hours per week, while the maximum working hours for workers are 40 hours per week. Therefore, the working hours of machines will be more than twice that of employees. (29th day, National Telegraph)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Woodin declared that the government will issue public bonds of 5 billion yuan for the economic recovery plan. To facilitate public cooperation, some of the public bonds will have very low face values, only 50 yuan per bond. (29th day, Havas Telegraph)

(Washington) The National Association of Manufacturers today proposed an important issue concerning President Roosevelt's movement to increase the purchasing power of American labor. The association decided to ask its members not to sign automatic blank regulations for the time being. (These regulations stipulate the working hours and wages for industries that have not submitted their own satisfactory regulations.) They must wait until they find out how those in charge of implementing the national recovery plan will handle workers whose existing wages are higher than the minimum but whose weekly working hours are longer than those stipulated in the regulations before they can sign blank regulations. The association said that if a clause in the regulations, a joint clause, stipulates that workers paid by the hour must be paid wages according to the reduced weekly price for their reduced working hours, many industrial contracts will be unsustainable. American industries have supported business and suffered losses for the past three years. Those whose finances are exhausted are counted by the year. Now, they cannot bear the increased labor costs without higher prices and wider sales. Those who have shorter working hours should have their wages increased appropriately by means of equal adjustment. According to official opinion, if this regulation is turned into a tool for reducing higher wages in order to divide the work so as to compensate for lower wages, it would run counter to the original intention of the regulation. Therefore, it is expected that workers with higher wages will be given equal adjustments in wages to compensate for their fewer working hours. (29th day, Reuters)

Tens of Thousands of Hollywood Workers Go on Strike 21

The World Economic Conference Failed, and War Debt Negotiations Stalled 23

(Washington) Now That the World Economic Conference Has Come to Nothing, Public Opinion Here Also Expresses Great Doubt About Whether the Issue of War Debts Can Proceed Smoothly, Although the US President Intends to Discuss a Revised War Debt Repayment Schedule With Representatives of the Debtor Nations, Those Outside the White House Have Already Frankly Acknowledged That Negotiations Will Be in Vain, Because the Position of the United States Today Can No Longer Provide Anything as Compensation for Debt Repayment. Before the London Conference, It Was Widely Believed That After the United States Reduced Tariffs, It Could Make It Easier for Debtor Nations to Repay Their Debts, and the Debtor Nations Themselves Also Declared That When the United States Built High Tariff Walls, It Could No Longer Hope to Repay War Debts, Now That the London Conference Has Failed to Reduce Tariffs, Coupled With the Fact That the US President's Industrial Recovery Plan Will Increase Tariffs When Necessary to Protect Domestic Agriculture and Industry and Prevent Foreign Goods From Competing, the US President Still Holds the Power to Increase or Decrease Tariffs After Investigating the Cost of Production at Home and Abroad, It Is No Longer Possible to Guarantee a Reduction in Tariffs. This Situation Has Also Been Discussed by the Diplomatic Community Here, and No Remedy Has Been Found, but It Is Not Attributed to the US President, Acknowledging That the US Government Has Made It Easier for Debtor Nations to Repay Their Debts After Depreciating the Value of the Gold Dollar, However, on the Part of the Debtor Nations, Due to the Sudden Passage of the Industrial Recovery Act by the US Congress, It Is No Longer Possible to Sell More Goods in the US and Raise Funds to Repay Debts. Therefore, at the Beginning of This Month, It Was Widely Expected That the US President Would Launch War Debt Negotiations Immediately After Returning to the Capital, but One Month Has Passed Without Any Movement. The President's Planned Trip to His Hometown in New York State, Including Whether He Invited Diplomatic Representatives of the Debtor Nations to Talk at Hyde Park, Has Not Been Expressed by People in the White House. (29th day, National Telegraph)

Japan's Ministry of Foreign Affairs Holds Meetings for Days to Establish Diplomatic Foundations 25

Temporarily Adopting a Wait-and-See Attitude Towards China (Tokyo) Foreign Minister Uchida and Other Key Officials of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Have Held Head Meetings for Days to Study Diplomatic Policies to Cope With the World Economic War After the Failure of the Economic Conference and the Amendment to the Naval Treaty at the Washington Conference and the London Conference in 1935. Now, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Has Largely Decided to Take the Following Diplomatic Guidelines as Its Foundation: (1) Policy Towards China: Japan Will Always Maintain a Self-Determined and Tough Attitude Towards China in Accordance With Established Guidelines, Resolutely Reject All Aid Plans of the League of Nations and the United Kingdom and the United States to China, and Strive to Make China Automatically Recognize the True Meaning of the Monroe Doctrine of the East; (2) Trade Policy: After the Failure of the Economic Conference, the World Economic War Will Inevitably Intensify, and the Attack on Japan by Countries Around the World Will Be Particularly Fierce. Japan Should Consider Self-Defense Measures Against This, While Actively Adopting the Policy of Developing Overseas Markets for Japanese Goods, That Is, First Concluding Reciprocal Trade Treaties With Countries That Have Close Relations, While Actively Taking Retaliatory Measures Against Countries That Suppress Japanese Trade, and Opening Up Markets in Africa, India, the South Pacific, Central America, and South America in the Shortest Possible Time in Order to Develop Japan's Foreign Trade; (3) General International Policy: Since Japan Withdrew From the League of Nations, Although it Has Resumed an Independent Diplomatic Policy, it Should Adopt a Compromising Policy in Negotiations With Various Countries. Therefore, Embassies Will Be Established in Egypt, South Africa, Afghanistan, Colombia, and Ethiopia, and New International Cultural Bureaus Will Be Established to Strive to Enhance Cultural Relations With Various Countries; (4) Policy Towards the Washington Conference in 1935: At the Washington Conference in 1935, Japan Demands Equality Between Japan's Naval Power and That of the United Kingdom and the United States. The Conference Will Definitely Discuss General Pacific Issues Such as the Issue of China's International Management [Manchukuo], in Order to Implement the Reasonable Claims of the Japanese Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Has Established a Research Department as a Staff Agency to Study Fundamental Countermeasures. (30th day, Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) The New Director of the Asian Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Kuwashima, Visited Foreign Minister Uchida, Vice Minister Shigemitsu, Director of the European and American Bureau Togo, Director of the Treaty Bureau Kuriyama, and Others at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the Morning of the 29th to Report on the Current Situation in North China and Exchange Views on Policy Towards China. As a Result, it Was Decided That Japan Would Continue to Adopt a Quiet Observation Policy Towards China, That Is, Since China Filed the Sino-Japanese Issue With the League of Nations, It Has Seemed to Have No Pro-Japanese Attitude, but Has Concluded Contracts With the United States and European Countries to Borrow Money or Import Weapons, and Has Cooperated With the League of Nations to Adopt Anti-Japanese Policies. At This Time, Japan's Strong Talk of an Asian Alliance With China Will Definitely Have No Results, so We Will Temporarily Continue to Adopt a Quiet Observation Policy and Establish a Policy Towards China at an Appropriate Time. (30th day, Japan United Press)

China Cooperates With the League of Nations 26

U.S.-Soviet Resumption of Diplomatic Relations 29

Rapid Developments: According to a Paris dispatch on the 29th, U.S. banker Baruch, a close friend of President Roosevelt, is currently traveling in Europe for personal matters. According to a Havas dispatch from New York on the 29th, discussions regarding the restoration of commercial relations between the U.S. and the Soviet Union have made rapid progress. It is now reported that the Soviet government has decided to purchase industrial equipment worth $75 million from the U.S. A delegation of 41 technicians has been dispatched to study the status of industrial equipment and select the industrial equipment most needed by the Soviet Union, such as industrial machinery, aircraft, aircraft parts, kerosene, drilling machines, automobiles, and cotton. It is reported that the China Good Offices Loan Corporation will provide further loans to the Soviet Union to purchase American cotton. According to reports, most of the industrial equipment the Soviet Union wants to purchase was previously supplied by Germany. The U.S. is currently negotiating long-term loans to the Soviet Union to allow American industrialists to compete with the Germans. Nine million dollars of this loan is to be used to purchase machinery for manufacturing thin metal sheets, and one million dollars will be used to purchase various agricultural and industrial tools.

Regulations on Telegraph Savings 40

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has newly revised the regulations on telegraph savings. Arabic numerals can be used to write addresses, house numbers, and various numbers. Parentheses should be placed before and after the numbers. In plain language, four Arabic numerals are counted as one word for charging. In code language, five numbers are counted as one word. The Japanese Military Makes Things Difficult for the Takeover of War Zones: 51

Yao, Ri: The Japanese Military Forces the Security Team to Roll Call in Tangshan, and Openly Makes Unreasonable Demands. Special Dispatch from Tianjin: From the Signing of the Tanggu Truce to Our Side Taking Over the War Zones, Two Months Have Passed. During These Two Months, the Takeover Committee Members Have Been Running Around in the Heat, and Their Situation is Very Difficult. However, the Result of the Takeover is an "Incomplete" Showing, and an Achievement of "Humiliating Patience." This Takeover is Divided into Two Routes: The Eastern Route Consists of Eleven Counties (in Reality, Dushan County is Not Included), and the Northern Route Only Consists of Five Counties (in Reality, Xinglong County is Not Included). The Eastern Route is an Area Where the Japanese and Puppet Armies are Concentrated, and the Situation is Complicated. The Takeover Committee Members Who Believe Optimistically are Blinded by the Situation. Taking Linyu County, Which is Full of Conflicts and Complications, as an Example, Before Liu Shisun Went to Shanhaiguan to Negotiate, He Said That There Were No Problems, and Ordered County Magistrate Yin Shousong to Accompany Him. This Was Like a Bolt From the Blue, Which Could Make the Takeover Committee Members Sing a Sentence: "Cold Water Poured on the Head, Embracing Ice!" Therefore, Yin Tong Became Very Anxious and Visited Yu Xuezhong, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, Who Still Advocated That the Takeover Personnel Should Proceed as Usual and Not Give Up Because of a Minor Setback. Then, He Took a Special Train to Beiping to Report to Huang Fu and Rushed Back to Tianjin That Night. The Next Morning, He Led the County Magistrates, Public Security Bureau Chiefs, and Auxiliary Personnel to Depart on Two Trains. The Security Team That Boarded the Train at the Tianjin East Station Consisted of 145 People on the First Train and 189 People on the Second Train. When the Special Train Passed Junliangcheng, 2,000 Newly Organized Security Team Members Boarded the Train. They Were All Fully Armed and Attached With Many Light Machine Guns. However, the Security Team Members Were Riding in Open Cars Without Protection From Wind and Rain. The Source of This Security Team is a Reorganized Army, and We Do Not Need to Say It Outright, Because the Japanese Have Already Investigated and Understood It Clearly. The Japanese Regard These Non-Resistant Soldiers as Rotten Wood. Now, Even Though They Have Transformed Into Police, They are Even Less Worth Mentioning. Therefore, the Japanese Side Had No Objections to the Formation of This Security Team. Unexpectedly, the Weather Was Not Good, and It Started to Rain Heavily After the Two Trains Passed Beitang. The 2,000-Odd Security Team Members Stood Erect in the Open Cars, Receiving a Thorough Washing. On the Same Day, They Arrived in Tangshan at 11:00 AM, But the Rain Had Not Stopped. The Japanese Soldiers Prevented the Security Team From Getting Off the Train. At That Time, the Security Team Members' Clothes and Hats Were Soaked, and the Water in the Open Cars Was Up to Their Knees. Then, Takasaki, the Commander of the Railway Line Garrison of the Japanese Kwantung Army Stationed in Tangshan, Asked Yin Tong About the Number of Security Team Members and Weapons. Yin Immediately Asked Dou Xizhe, the Commander of the General Team, to Tell Him the Truth. Takasaki Immediately Ordered Them to Get Off the Train and Roll Call. Dou Xizhe Immediately Refused, Saying That He Had Already Rolled Call When They Boarded the Train, and There Was No Need to Bother Him Again. Takasaki Still Insisted on Getting Off the Train and Rolling Call. Yin Was Afraid That It Would Become a Deadlock and Wanted to Order the Security Team Members to Get Off the Train, Line Up, and Report Their Numbers. Dou, the Commander of the General Team, Insisted That This Was Not Possible. In the End, He Opened a List of Numbers and Gave It to Takasaki to Check the Number of People in Each Car and the Types of Guns in Detail and Record Them. Soon After, He Notified Yin Tong That the Train Taking Over the War Zones Must Leave Today at 1:30 PM and Designated Tangshan, Luanzhou, Changli, and Linyu as the Disembarkation Points for the Takeover Personnel and the Security Team. They Were Not Allowed to Get Off the Train Except at the Designated Locations. His Attitude Was Arrogant and Intimidating, Treating Us Like a Protected Nation. I Don't Know How Those Who Were Bearing the Brunt Could Endure It. However, There Were Even More Embarrassing Things. The Takeover Personnel Went to Jiaotong University in the Rain, Where They Were Introduced to Li Jichun by Xue Zhiheng and Lei Shourong. Then, They Were Introduced to Song Yeowei, the So-Called Commander of the Japanese Army Stationed in Tangshan of the Northern Ning Railway Garrison Team (I Heard He Was a Detachment Commander). Song Yeowei Immediately Issued a Paper Printed by Wax Paper to Each County Magistrate, Entitled "Matters Required of County Magistrates and Public Security Bureau Chiefs." The Original Text is as Follows:

(1) Regarding All Administrative Procedures, I Hope That You Will Strictly Abide By the Agreement on the Ceasefire Between China and Japan.

(2) When Each County Magistrate and Public Security Bureau Chief Takes Office, Please Report the Following Matters to Our Team as Soon as Possible (Turn to Commander Song Yeowei in the 14th Mixed Brigade in Shanhaiguan): 1. The Announcement (Two Copies) of Each County Magistrate Taking Office Should Be Sent to Our Team as Soon as Possible (All Announcements Afterwards Should Be Reported Immediately); 2. The Announcement (Two Copies) of Each Public Security Bureau Chief Taking Office Should Be Sent to Our Team as Soon as Possible (All Announcements Afterwards Should Be Reported Immediately); 3. The Arrangement of the Public Security Bureau (Namely, Address, Number of People, Number of Horses, Types of Weapons (Guns), and the Number of Each); 4. The Arrangement of the Police (Namely, Address, Number of People, Number of Horses, Types of Weapons (Guns), and the Number of Each); 5. The Situation of the Local Self-Defense Corps and the Actual Number of Guns].

After Reading the Above Notice, Each Takeover Personnel Was Silent and Made No Expression, Not Knowing Whether They Rejected It or Accepted It. The Reporter Asked Yu Xuezhong, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, for His Opinion on This. Yu Said, "I Always Seek Thoroughness in Handling Affairs. Regarding the Takeover Issue, I Have Always Advocated That All Conflicts and Obstacles Should Be Resolved Thoroughly, and That We Cannot Prevaricate and Accept It Vaguely. The Notice Sent by Song Yeowei to the Takeover Personnel is a Disregard for China's Sovereignty. If It is Reported to the Provincial Government, I Will Completely Reject It." The Special Train for the Takeover Still Drove East From Tangshan at the Limited Time of Takasaki. The Rain Was Getting Heavier. It Arrived in Luanzhou at 3:30 PM. County Magistrate Zhang, Public Security Bureau Chief Meng Xuehan, Leting County Magistrate Guan Gengyu, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Zhigang, and the Security Team Got Off the Train. The Special Train Stopped for Three Hours. The Small Japanese Officer Still Inquired Several Times in the Rain. It Arrived in Changli at 8:00 PM. County Magistrate Liang, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Gang, Dou Xizhe, the Commander of the Security General Team, and the Security Team All Got Off the Train. The Special Train Was Originally Intended to Continue Driving East, But Unexpectedly, the Staff of the Puppet Fengshan Railway Deliberately Made Things Difficult and Did Not Give Them the Road Ticket, So They Could Not Drive the Train. At This Time, There Were Still Thousands of Security Team Members Who Had Not Gotten Off the Train. They Were Exposed to the Wind and Rain and Had Not Eaten for a Day. They Were Already Exhausted. Fortunately, After County Magistrate Liang, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang, and Dou, the Commander of the General Team, Got Off the Train, They Quickly Found a Way to Send Boiled Water, Large Flatbreads, Steamed Buns, and Pickles to Satisfy Their Hunger and Relieve Their Suffering. However, They Could Not Get Off the Train, So They Had No Place to Stay, and They Could Not Change Their Wet Clothes. The Next Morning (the 28th) at 4:00 AM, the Special Train Drove East From Changli. At 5:00 AM, It Arrived in Liushouying. Funing County Magistrate Liu Xingpei, Public Security Bureau Chief Song Ziyou, Lulong County Magistrate Chen Zengshi, Public Security Bureau Chief Xu Fugui, and the Security Team Got Off the Train. At 6:00 AM, It Arrived in Qinhuangdao. At This Time, the Clouds Had Dispersed and the Sky Was Clear, and the Sea Breeze Was Assaulting People, Giving a Great Sense of Autumn. Yin Tong and Yin Shousong Got Off the Train to Contact the Japanese Garrison Headquarters. It So Happened That the Northern Ning Railway Bureau Heard That the Special Train Was Being Obstructed a Lot, So It Also Sent Section Chief Liu to Take a Passenger Car to Catch Up and Negotiate to Drive the Train East. At 7:00 AM, It Arrived in Shanhaiguan. As Soon as the Special Train Pulled Into the Station Platform, a Team of Japanese Military Police and a Team of Puppet State Police Fully Armed Surrounded the Special Train with a Fierce Momentum, Not Allowing the Security Team to Get Off the Train and Wanting to Confiscate Their Weapons. After Several Negotiations, It Was Ultimately Ineffective. Yin Tong, Liu Shisun, Yin Shousong, and Others Went to Visit Naka River, the Commander of the Japanese Army Garrisoning in Yuguan. Naka River Actually Said That the Shanhaiguan Railway Station Already Belonged to the Territory of Manchuria. He Had Not Received an Order Here and Could Not Allow Armed People to Get Off the Train Here. He Hoped That Your Team Would Withdraw Quickly. Moreover, the Linyu County Government Office Has Already Been Moved to Haiyang Town, and Shanhaiguan is No Longer Under the Jurisdiction of Linyu County. Yin, Liu, and Others Went to Visit Hattori Heiji郎, Commander of the 14th Mixed Brigade of the Japanese Army, and His Staff Officer Yazaki. Hattori Expressed It Even More Wonderfully, Saying That Your Place Can Take Over Linyu County Without Any Problems. You Can Go to Haiyang Town to Take Over. However, Shanhaiguan City Has Been Delineated Into the Borderline of Manchuria. There Are Many Troops Stationed Here, and I am Afraid That There Will Be Inconveniences. Apart From This Place, You Can Move Linyu County to Any Place You Want, and I am Willing to Send Commander Naka River to Accompany County Magistrate Yin to Haiyang Town to Take Over. If There Are Any Obstacles, I Am Willing to Be Responsible for Resolving Them. Therefore, the Special Train Returned to Qinhuangdao. It Was Heard That It Was Scheduled to Leave This Morning (the 29th) at 9:00 AM With Naka River Leading a Team of Japanese Soldiers to Accompany County Magistrate Yin and Public Security Bureau Chief Huang Tianmin to Take Over. Whether There Are Any Obstacles, the Provincial Government Has Not Received a Report Until 3:00 PM This Afternoon. However, the Puppet State's Border Guard Line is Set Up at the Shi River, Dividing the Boundaries. People Entering This Borderline Must Be Strictly Searched and Interrogated, and Their Whereabouts Must Be Recorded in Detail Before They Are Allowed to Pass. In the Future, It Will Be Difficult to Set Up the Linyu County Government in Shanhaiguan. It Was Heard That the Telegraph Bureau in Shanhaiguan City Has Been Changed Into a Japanese Restaurant. He Zhuguo's Police Garrison Headquarters Has Been Changed Into the Miyato Detachment of the Japanese Army. The Headquarters of the Hattori Brigade is Stationed in the Private Residence of the Richest Man in Linyu, the Tian Family. The South Gate Tower Has Been Swept Away by Artillery Fire. The Plaque of the First Pass in the World at the East Gate is Still Intact. The Linyu County Government Has Been Replaced by the Puppet Local Maintenance Association. The Girls' School Has Been Stopped, and the Boys' School Continues to Have Classes as Usual. There Are Many Bandits Lurking in the Northeast of the County City, Near the Great Wall. Although Our Security Team Stipulates That Tangshan Should Have Three Squads, Changli, Linyu, and Qian'an Should Each Have Two Squads, and the Remaining Counties Should Each Have One Squad, Qian'an is Still Controlled by the Japanese and Puppet Regime. There is No Definite News on When the Takeover Will Take Place. Even If the Takeover Takes Place in the Future, It Is Very Close to Lengkou, Which Means That the Bandits With a Background are Not Something That Two Security Squads Can Handle. We Are Very Worried About the Change of Power in Linyu and Qian'an. The Counties That Are Currently Taking Over Smoothly Are Only Luan County, Changli, Fengrun, Leting, Yutian, and Ninghe, etc. However, the People of Ninghe Have Mostly Fled, and the County Government Office Has Been Destroyed and Cannot Work. The County Magistrate, Yuan Shibin, Intends to Submit a Request to the Provincial Government to Temporarily Set Up a Government Office in Lutai to Work. (July 29th)

Zhao Qilu's Impeachment Case 54

A dispatch from Zhenjiang regarding the Jiangsu Provincial Government's appeal to the Government Council: Zhao Qilu, the Director of Civil Affairs of Jiangsu Province, was impeached by Supervisory Committee member Liu San. The Secretariat of the National Government's Disciplinary Committee for Political Officials sent a letter to Director Zhao. In addition to submitting a defense to the committee within the specified time limit, Zhao also submitted the 588th committee report of the provincial government. The report concluded that the provincial government should thoroughly investigate the case, provide a detailed account of the facts, and submit it to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, as well as send a letter to the Disciplinary Committee clarifying the truth and responsibilities. The aforementioned submissions were sent separately on the 28th of this month. The original text is divided into four points, totaling approximately six thousand words. The gist of it is that the accusations in the impeachment document against Zhao Qilu, the Director of Civil Affairs of Jiangsu Province, are not only completely contrary to the facts but also illogical. The criticisms can be roughly divided into four points. In summary, the provincial government has a consistent policy regarding the appointment and removal of officials, and the punishment of corruption is carried out in accordance with the central government's intentions. All procedures and processes involved are jointly discussed and decided upon by the provincial government's committee and reported to the Executive Yuan and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. The case files are available for review. Director Zhao, as a member of the provincial committee, is only carrying out orders and should not be held solely responsible. However, the impeachment document states that the selection of county magistrates caused social resentment, that the reluctance to easily replace county magistrates induced them to retain their positions, that the punishment of corrupt county magistrates violated the law, and that the promotion of outstanding personnel was undeserved. This implies that the provincial government's actions regarding the appointment, removal, reward, and punishment of county magistrates are all unacceptable. This raises the question of how officials can fulfill their duties and what other paths they should take to be considered legitimate. This is not only impossible in reality but also illogical. Furthermore, it is noted that Supervisory Committee member Liu filed the impeachment based on Wang Qinghe's false accusations, and the Supervisory Yuan's request for disciplinary action was based on the reports of secret investigators. The Director of Civil Affairs is a key national appointee, and violating the law is a serious charge of dereliction of duty. To allow impeachment based on Wang Qinghe's baseless accusations and secret investigators' reports that contradict the facts would set a precedent that would make officials constantly vulnerable to insult and harm. False accusers could freely disrupt and slander without fear, leading to the reversal of right and wrong, the confusion of black and white, and the decline of morality. What kind of government system would that be?

Declaration by Important Communist Party Member Cai Jiantang and Others 55

Exposing the Mistakes and Crimes of the Communist Party Based on Awareness, They Joined the Kuomintang: Seven people, including Cai Jiantang, former secretary of the Central Military Commission of the Communist Party, issued an anti-communist declaration. The original text is as follows:

What is Gained by Fumbling in the Dark Will Always Be Darkness: The Chinese Communist Party is only fumbling and proceeding in the dark. Its ultimate end will only be to create more mistakes and crimes, until it meets its fate of decline and death. We were all once loyal members of the Chinese Communist Party. Now we have resolutely converted to the brilliant banner of the Three Principles of the People. This is not a contradiction or a betrayal of class. This is the harvest we have gained from a painful recollection of fumbling in the dark. This marks the beginning of a new era in our life history.

Our transformation is not accidental. It is based on understanding several fundamental issues:

1. What Kind of Country is China? 56

No one can deny that China is an economically backward country. In a poor and weak country, there are only the very poor and the less poor. There is no fundamental class antagonism to speak of. This basic understanding is enough to defeat Marx's theory of class struggle without residue. Communism, which is not suitable for China's national conditions, has been brought to China, resulting in China becoming even more poor and weak. It cannot create production, but rather destroys production. In fact, this is the case. The Chinese Communist Party has never done any work to create production. It has completely devoted itself to the violent acts of destroying production.

2. Do We Need National Rejuvenation or Fundamentally Reject National Concepts? 57

Whether it is the Italian nation, the Germanic nation, the Yamato nation, or even the Slavic nation, these self-improving nations have all been able to develop national self-confidence and national independence. Looking back at our Chinese nation, it is like a plate of loose sand, precisely the result of a lack of national self-confidence and national independence. At present, China's national crisis is very serious. Uniting together to resist Japan is the only good plan to save China and rejuvenate the nation. However, the Chinese Communist Party has proposed the opposition of the lower-level united front and the national united front, such as instigating anti-Japanese soldiers to kill anti-Japanese officers. The heroic sacrifice and bloody battles around the Great Wall were originally for the survival of the nation, but the Communist Party exhausted its ability to sabotage the rear, even colluding with the Japanese side to contain anti-Japanese military operations. The madness of the Chinese Communist Party shows that it has no national concept, and everything is based on the will of the Slavic nation. Without a national concept, how can one speak of revolution? It is simply a parasite of the Chinese nation.

3. Is the Initial Victory in One or Several Provinces Feudal Separatism? 58

China is currently facing an extremely serious national crisis. What is needed is the unity of national strength. Whoever tries to split national strength is the common enemy of the Chinese nation. The central government is committed to resolving internal disputes in order to overcome the national crisis. Anyone who hinders the unity of national strength will be given the central government's painstaking consideration in order to find a political solution. During this period of national crisis, the Chinese Communist Party may not want to resist Japan, but the Soviet territory of one or several provinces cannot be given up. Their destruction of unity is the same as general feudal separatism. However, its danger is more than ten or a hundred times greater. The Northeast has fallen to Japanese imperialism, and success in the Soviet territory is tantamount to being a dependency of Soviet Russia.

4. Is the Chinese Communist Party Increasingly Developing or Increasingly Collapsing? 59

From the speculation of the erroneous political line of the Chinese Communist Party, it can be affirmed that it will inevitably collapse. From the current situation of the Chinese Communist Party, it can be proved that this affirmation is completely correct. Lines are changed one after another, mistakes are constantly repeated, and the needs of the Chinese revolution are not understood at all. Of course, they will be indecisive and eventually become unmanageable. The Chinese Communist Party, despite its arbitrary propaganda and chanting of the arrival of the revolutionary climax, is actually only deceiving itself. Reviewing the Communist Party's activities over the years, it has exhausted its disruptive role everywhere. The red areas are desolate, the huts are kilns, and the rural economy is completely bankrupt. Even in non-red areas, it has exerted its destructive means. However, once poisoned by the Communist Party, the public's hatred of the Communist Party has deepened, and the Communist Party's organizational strength has been weakened. This is the inevitable result of its political bankruptcy. The Shanghai Party, which the Communist Party boasts as being advanced, is not only pitifully weak in organization, but also most of the workers, the so-called class of the Communist Party itself, are unwilling to be used by it. However, the Communist Party insists that it is confident in winning over the majority of workers. The development of the organization, the September 18th and January 28th calls, with party members claiming four or five thousand, are nothing more than desperate struggles and bluster. The actual number of party members is less than several hundred. The mass base is even more unknown. Defection of party members has become a trend, leaving the Communist Party with nothing to do but cover up its collapsing state. The ironclad facts are clearly laid out before people. The Chinese Communist Party has embarked on the road to death.

5. Who is the Sole Leader of the Chinese Revolution? 60

The road of the Bolsheviks, the facts tell us that this road is impassable. There is no doubt that only the Three Principles of the People can save China at present. The Three Principles of the People instruct us that national self-determination is needed to break away from the status of a semi-colonial country, that we must establish a truly popular revolutionary regime, and that we must solve the people's livelihood problems in accordance with China's national conditions, with the correct method of regulating capital and equalizing land rights. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood repeatedly explained the morbid Marxist theory and established the philosophical basis of the historical view of the people's livelihood. We firmly believe that only the great Three Principles of the People is the only doctrine that can save China, and the Chinese Kuomintang, which implements the revolution of the Three Principles of the People, is the only revolutionary party that leads the Chinese revolution.

Recognizing the current stage of history and advancing along the axis of history, we have resolutely transformed from the camp of the Bolsheviks to the banner of the Three Principles of the People. We believe that this is a great transformation.

We deeply know that the comrades of the Chinese Communist Party and the Communist Youth League who are still wandering in the dark are full of pain and feel that there is no way out. We earnestly hope that they will quickly transform from a political and personal bloody lesson and bravely stand on the front line of the Three Principles of the People's revolution, and work together towards a bright future. Cai Jiantang, Xian Daqi, Du Yueying, Wang Lubing, Xu Xian, Zhao Yingchun, He Bengen. July 24th.

Lu and Han Order County Magistrates Along the River to Move to the Embankment to Supervise Construction 61

They May Not Return to the County Without Approval: A dispatch from Jinan reports that when the Yellow River surged last year and the situation was precarious, Chairman Han Fuju, in order to protect the lives and property of millions of people along the river, ordered the county magistrates along the river to move to the embankment to supervise the construction. All officers and soldiers and laborers worked together, and fortunately, the river was safe. This year, the danger of the Yellow River is even greater than last year. As of recently, the river has been rising wildly, and the water level is not much different from the highest water level last year, and in some places, it has exceeded it. Because the water source is still strong, it is expected that there will be a large surge around the beginning of autumn. In addition to the River Affairs Bureau raising the embankment and supervising the officers and soldiers to repair it, Chairman Han today also ordered the twenty-two county magistrates along the river to move to the embankment immediately due to the repeated rise in water and the tense construction situation. The county magistrates are ordered to supervise the laborers to work with the river workers and soldiers day and night to protect the embankment, so as to ensure that there is no danger. They must be stationed at the construction site for at least one week. If the water recedes and the construction is stable, they may return to the county after submitting a report for approval. The river water situation is slightly stable today (July 28th). The upstream Lishangtun has slightly decreased, the middle reaches have increased, and the downstream water level is stable. Zhang Lianjia, director of the River Affairs Bureau, and Zhao Luren, chief of the General Affairs Section, went to Luokou by car this morning to inspect the river construction situation and returned in the afternoon. According to them, the water situation is still stable, and although the water is large in the middle reaches, there is no change. The water level table for each section of the river today is as follows: Lishangtun in the upper reaches, down three centimeters, water level 58 meters 3 inches; Guanzhuang in the middle reaches up 1.2 centimeters, water level 35 meters 9 inches 1 point (exceeding the highest water level last year); Luokou up 1.5 centimeters, water level 30 meters 0 inches 5 points (only 5 centimeters lower than the highest water level last year); Scorpion Bay in the lower reaches, up 7 centimeters, water level 18 meters 2 inches 7 points; Dama House is level, water level 14 meters 3 inches. (July 28th)

Family Dispute in the Songjiang Xi Family Tragedy 62

In the tragic death case of Xi Yongda, the chairman of the Huayangqiao Xi Yongda Rice Shop, and his wife Tu Quanxi, the surviving young sons, Shichang and Shirong, are both minors. An ad hoc relatives' meeting was immediately established, and their maternal uncles, Tu Xinnong and Tu Wenjie, were appointed as guardians. Xi Weisheng, Xi Weibin, Xu Chunbo, and Shen Lichu were appointed as supervisors of the guardians. Gu Shouyi and Tu Heyun were hired as lawyers to manage the estate and provide legal protection for the two young sons. During this process, the guardian supervisor Xi Weibin tore up a promissory note for 2,000 yuan and made various threats, preventing the guardians from performing their duties. Furthermore, the previous day, a threatening letter signed "Qiyouzi One" was received, stating that after the deaths of Xi Weiquan and his wife, the post-mortem affairs should be managed by the Xi clan. However, because the two sons are young, a relatives' meeting has been formed, but it is only a formal guarantee. If outsiders want to participate, there is no shortage of people in Huayangqiao who are well aware of the matter, so there is no need for outside interference. If they still do not understand in the future, they will be dealt with in appropriate ways, so as not to involve Weiquan's son, who will follow in his father's footsteps, and that they are also quite dangerous, so they should let go as soon as possible. In order to protect the interests of the wards, the Tu brothers took the two sons home on the 25th and sent the boxes of documents to lawyer Gu for safekeeping in another place to avoid other changes. They also notified all members of the relatives' meeting. However, the guardian supervisor Xi Weisheng was very dissatisfied with this move, which was not discussed in advance and was a decisive action. He also entrusted lawyer Lu Longxiang to make a statement on his behalf. The dispute may be just beginning.

Salt Boats Robbed at Yangcheng Lake Mouth in Changshu 63

Liuhhe, Taicang, is a place where official salt is produced. A few days ago, the local Salt Guild had over ten thousand yuan of salt, which was divided into nine large boats and transported to Zhenjiang, Dantu, Yaojiaqiao, and other places for unloading. Unexpectedly, at around 10:00 on the 28th, the salt boats passed through Yangcheng Lake Mouth in the county, and one boat fell behind, resulting in a robbery. The boat was carrying a total of 1,050 packages of salt, of which more than 300 packages were robbed (each package priced at 6 yuan). When the bandits came, they were on two boats, carrying about twenty bandits, all in white shirts and yellow trousers, and holding four box guns and many rifles. After the incident, the boat crew landed and reported the robbery to the Xiangcheng District Office to request an arrest. Although the security regiment dispatched to search, they found nothing. Currently, two of the boat crew members are injured and have been admitted to Xiangcheng Hospital.

Stealing Watermelons Leads to Murder in Changzhou 65

Bai Ruilin, a farmer in Zhangjia Village near Zhahe Bridge west of Wuyi County, has several acres of melon fields, and his eighteen-year-old eldest son, Zhang Tinggen, watches the melons in the fields day and night. Unexpectedly, Wu Zhaorong and Wu Pangliu, villagers in the same village, went to steal melons during the day and were spotted by Zhang Tinggen, who confronted them. Wu and others not only did not admit it, but beat Tinggen, hitting his vital point, causing him to be seriously injured and fall to the ground. His father found out and carried him back for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died on the evening of the 28th. Bai Ruilin was saddened by the death of his son. In addition to handing over the two murderers to the local bailiff for custody, he submitted a report to the county court on the 29th. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongyi went to the countryside on the 30th to conduct an autopsy.

In the past few days, the canal water level at the Qingjiangpu main gate of the Huai-Pi section of the canal has been increasing daily. Its water level has exceeded the highest level of last year by more than three feet. The canal flood is quite worrying. On the 29th, the Qingjiang Main Gate rose another 1 foot 1 inch.

Guiding Light, a Child Bride Commits Suicide 68

Yang Wu, a peddler living in Houshan Village, had a widowed son of fifteen years old, engaged a Sun girl as his daughter in law and was child rearing for a long time. The girl, although sixteen, looked like an adult. Yesterday (28th), while Yang and others were out, she suddenly hanged herself in the room. When Yang arrived, she was already dead.

The First National Government Construction Lottery Will Be Drawn Today 69

At one o'clock this afternoon, a plane will scatter flowers at Yiyuan to welcome the public for free viewing. The top prize will definitely be drawn from sold numbers. Starting from the 8th, the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery, handled by the Central, China, and Communications Banks, will be drawn in public at Yiyuan on Albert Road in the French Concession at 1:00 PM today. There will be quite a lively scene. According to the announcement, there are 667 winning numbers from the first prize to the seventh prize, which will take about seven hours to draw completely. In order to save time, all ceremonies will be simplified. Approximately after the China National Aviation Corporation sends a specially assigned plane to the arena to scatter flowers and colored streamers, the lottery will begin. The Yiyuan address is large and can accommodate more than 10,000 spectators. The Construction Lottery is related to national construction. The lottery office will not pre-issue admission tickets for the first lottery drawing, and welcomes people from all walks of life to come to the arena to watch freely and participate in the grand event together. Furthermore, the lottery prizes were originally scheduled to be paid directly by the lottery office. In order to facilitate the prize winners to collect their prizes, the office has specially entrusted the Central, China, and Communications Banks, and their branches in various places, to handle the payment on their behalf. The effective period for prize payment is from August 8th of this year to January 31st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. It is also reported that the Ministry of Finance, because a portion of the first lottery tickets has not yet been sold out, in order to maintain the rights of the ticket buyers and consolidate national credit, the government has specially approved that the first prize must be drawn from the sold lottery ticket numbers. The method is as follows: If the first prize is first drawn from the sold lottery ticket numbers, there is no problem. If the first prize is first drawn from the lottery ticket numbers retained by the Ministry of Finance, in addition to issuing the prize money for the last two digits and the last one digit that are the same as this number, the government will give up the 500,000 yuan first prize money that this number itself should have received, and give it to the ticket buyers. After all the prizes have been drawn today, another drawing will be held on the spot. In any case, it will be drawn from the sold lottery ticket numbers. However, the prize money for the last two digits or one digit that are the same will still be issued in accordance with the first prize number.

Li Jingcong Returns to Shanghai to Talk 70

The Qinghai Branch Line Will Be Tested Next Month, and the Eurasian Joint Flight is Still Undetermined. Li Jingcong, General Manager of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, returned to Shanghai by plane yesterday after going to Beiping due to his mother's illness. According to him, the Northwest Aviation Qinghai Branch Line has now been changed to depart for a test flight in the middle of next month (August). He was unable to conduct the test flight as scheduled last time because he returned to Beiping to visit his parents due to his mother's illness. Now that his mother's illness has slightly improved, he immediately returned to Shanghai. After making some arrangements in Shanghai, he will depart in the middle of next month. As for the implementation of the Eurasia joint flight, there are no problems on the foreign side. The only difference is that if there are no problems on the domestic side, it can be started at any time. Also, the entire line between Shanghai and Dihua is about 4,000 kilometers long, and the round-trip flights have excellent results. The route between Dihua and Tacheng is only 500 kilometers. There is no problem in implementing joint flights. The problem on the domestic side is the communication of Dihua's radio. If Dihua's radio can communicate, there will be no other problems in the future, and the joint flight can be realized. Therefore, before the problems on the domestic route are resolved, it is difficult to determine when the joint flight can begin. The statement that it will begin on August 1st is completely unfounded.

Preparing to Build a Large Oriental Port 71

The First Sounding Work is Completed: A Central News Agency report states that the preparations for the construction of a large oriental port have been carried out by the Preparatory Committee for the Construction of a Large Oriental Port, together with the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, to sound the seabed topography and coastline. The first sounding work has been completed. In order to expedite and complete this work, re-sounding has now begun. After the re-sounding is completed, three more soundings are required to produce a blueprint, which will be studied before construction begins. However, according to the sounders, the port is subject to very large waves due to its location, which has a significant impact on the berthing of ships. Therefore, it is necessary to build a breakwater to reduce the force of the waves.

Overseas Chinese Face Oppression 72

Distressed Overseas Chinese in Mexico Urgently Need Relief: Overseas Chinese in Japan Will Return to China on a Regular Basis: Mexico has been affected by the global economic downturn, resulting in a gradual increase in domestic unemployment. Seeing that overseas Chinese in China run small and medium-sized businesses and occupy a dominant position, they have disregarded diplomatic relations between the two countries and organized an anti-Chinese party to exclude overseas Chinese, rob property, and expel them. The distressed overseas Chinese who have been expelled back to China in succession are in twelve batches, about 2,000 people. There are still more than 10,000 people who cannot return to China due to a lack of travel funds. At the same time, overseas Chinese in Osaka, Nagasaki, and other places in Japan have been excluded, resulting in unemployment. They will return to China on a regular basis. The details are as follows:

U.S. Authorities Stop Funding 73

According to Peng Canguang, the general manager of the Overseas Chinese General Association, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, when Chinese overseas Chinese in Mexico were unable to bear the oppression, they all smuggled into the United States. The U.S. authorities knew that the Chinese overseas Chinese were refugees and were extremely generous, issuing each person 100 U.S. dollars for travel expenses to send them back to China. The distressed overseas Chinese relied on this to return to their homeland. Recently, as the anti-Chinese wave in Mexico is still fierce, the number of overseas Chinese fleeing into the United States is still on the way. In order to make up for the losses, it has negotiated with the Mexican government to bear the travel expenses, but it has been rejected. Therefore, the U.S. authorities immediately ordered the border police to stop the smuggling of overseas Chinese to avoid huge and undeserved losses.

Overseas Chinese in Mexico in a Dilemma 74

Since the U.S. government ordered a ban on smuggling, there are now tens of thousands of distressed overseas Chinese in a dilemma. They have no way to escape and no way to appeal. If no measures are taken to provide relief as soon as possible, they will be stranded in a foreign country. The consequences are unimaginable. Although the government has remitted 50,000 yuan to the minister in Mexico to provide assistance, it is a drop in the bucket and not enough to distribute. It is hoped that the government authorities will continue to provide assistance to save the innocent. According to Peng, a report has been received that more than 70 distressed overseas Chinese who entered the country before the ban on smuggling were detained and have been approved by the U.S. government to be sent back to China. However, the date of departure is still unknown.

Overseas Chinese in Japan Will Return to China on a Regular Basis 75

Since the September 18th Incident, Chinese overseas Chinese in Japan have been subjected to exclusion by the Japanese side. Recently, the anti-Chinese wave in Dalian, Nagasaki, and other places has been even worse than before, resulting in a large number of overseas Chinese being forced to lose their jobs. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has decided to welcome the overseas Chinese back to China to avoid being stranded. The Ministry of Finance has allocated 7,000 yuan to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to handle the relief matters. It is learned that there are currently about 300 overseas Chinese in Nagasaki, who are scheduled to return to China on the Changxing Company's Queen Asia Wheel on the 11th of next month. It is expected that they will arrive at the port on the 13th. Most of the above-mentioned overseas Chinese are from Fujian, Guangdong, and North China provinces. After arriving in Shanghai, they will be sent back to their places of origin separately.

It is said that the French envoy will stay in Beijing briefly and return to Shanghai at the end of this week.

Ministry of Industries to Formulate a Plan to Deal with Trade with Russia 78

Planning to Organize an Inspection Group and Set Up a Special Bureau Based on the Principle of Mutual Benefit and No Damage to Our Country's Commerce, According to New News Agency. The Soviet Russian government, in view of the increasingly busy commercial relations between the two countries since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, has specially sent Commercial Commissioner Komarov to China to investigate the state of our country's commerce as a reference for the development of Russian goods in the Chinese market. It also plans to establish a joint Sino-Russian commercial company in Tianjin with a capital of 8 million to 15 million yuan, specializing in import and export trade between the two countries. All these matters have been reported in the newspapers. A reporter from the New News Agency believes that the organization of this joint venture company is of great importance to the future of our country's trade with Russia, and therefore specially inquired of industrial circles and exporters for their opinions on this matter. All agreed that although there has been news of the Russian government sending Commercial Commissioner Komarov to China to investigate commerce, the industrial authorities have not yet received a formal report of when Komarov will depart from Russia. Therefore, it is not yet known whether he is being dispatched by the Russian government or is conducting a personal investigation. As for the establishment of a joint Sino-Russian commercial company in Tianjin, although no report has been received, this matter is of great importance to our entire trade. The Ministry of Industry has formulated a detailed plan to prepare for it, the principle of which is based on mutual benefit and no damage to our country's commerce. As for the official and commercial joint organization of a Soviet Russian industrial inspection group and the establishment of a special bureau for trade with Russia, the plans were temporarily delayed due to the incident of Soviet Russia selling the Chinese Eastern Railway. However, the Ministry of Industry is now doing its best to plan so that it can be realized as soon as possible, so that our country's trade with Russia can gradually develop and consolidate the foundation of competition.

Sichuan Native Place Association Presents Opinions on Sichuan Administration 79

Presented to the Government Authorities by Telegraph. The Sichuan Native Place Association in Shanghai recently sent a telegram to the government authorities, which read: Urgent. To Chairman Lin of Nanjing, Committee Chairman Jiang of Lushan, and President Wang, We humbly present our suggestions for eliminating the Sichuan war, which have been adopted by the authorities, demonstrating the government's concern for the western border. However, the Sichuan war has been going on for several days, and there is no hope for peace. The suffering of the people is becoming more and more urgent. Our association mourns the devastation of our homeland and the suffering of the people's livelihood, and therefore presents concrete measures to stabilize the situation in Sichuan. We earnestly request the government authorities to decide on and implement them during the Lushan Conference. It is well known that the Sichuan army is complex, there have been years of internal strife, Sichuan's administration is corrupt, and the people are living in misery. Therefore, the way to save Sichuan is to distinguish between the urgency of military, political, economic, and educational policies, and to set the essential measures to treat the symptoms and the root causes, and to order their implementation with the authority of the government, punishing violations with national law without any leniency, so that the future of Sichuan Province may have a glimmer of hope. First, the method of treating the symptoms in the military aspect is to unify command and streamline tactics. Please order the Bandit Suppression Commander Liu Xiang to lead the various armies to northern Sichuan to clear the communist bandits within a time limit to protect the people's livelihood and secure the villages. Also, order Liu Wenhui, the Pacification Commissioner of Sichuan and Xikang, to consolidate the Kangzang border defense and prevent the Dalai Lama from invading, so as to relieve the central government's concerns in the west. The method of treating the root cause is that Sichuan Province has 500,000 mercenaries and 2 million militia. After bandit suppression and border defense are completed, demobilization should begin. Except for a very small number of troops stationed in Chengdu, Chongqing, Kangding, and other places, the remaining soldiers should be demobilized. Local security should be the responsibility of the 2 million militia, which is more than sufficient. Second, the method of treating the symptoms in the political aspect is to break the defense zone system and carefully select the provincial chairman. If the defense zone is not broken, the division of territory will eventually become the source of all evils, which are difficult to eliminate. If the chairman is not carefully appointed to win the hearts of the people and seek the greatest happiness for our 70 million people, then orders will not be issued from the provincial capital, and disputes will arise. The method of treating the root cause is to establish a provincial legislative body as soon as possible based on the National Reconstruction Program, organized by representatives of agricultural, industrial, commercial, academic, and other vocational groups, and various people's groups outside Sichuan, to supervise the administration, formulate the provincial constitution, and enter the path of true democracy. Third, the method of treating the symptoms in the economic aspect is to effectively abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies and prohibit the pre-collection of grain taxes. In recent years, Sichuan Province has experienced the most severe exploitation in ancient and modern times, both at home and abroad. According to the investigation of this association, the pre-collection of grain taxes is as many as thirteen times a year, and the exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies are as few as more than 20 types per county. Even the lowest-level peddlers and hawkers in society pay an average of more than 10 yuan per year. The communist surge is well-founded. The method of treating the root cause is to revitalize the rural economy and restore export trade. Today's Sichuan economy has become a phenomenon of having villages without agriculture and having imports without exports. The blood is dry and the bones are damaged. If we do not try our best to save it and revive the remnants, then Jiangxi's situation will be a matter of time. Fourth, the method of treating the symptoms in the educational aspect is to strictly select educational administrative personnel and increase national education funds. Education bureaucrats, warlords and academic tycoons should not lead the education bureau, because it will defile the sacred cause of the foundation of the country. The funding for national universities should be increased and used effectively to enrich the content of the highest institution of learning in the southwest. The method of treating the root cause is to make educational funding independent and implement universal education in various counties. The educational funding in Sichuan Province was originally set at more than 4 million from the meat tax of each county, but the military intercepted it, causing education to go bankrupt. In the future, it should be handed over to the Education Department for unified planning and expenditure. Although the implementation of universal education in various counties is more difficult, since Sichuan Province is large and rich, as long as the countryside is revived and exploitation is reduced, funding will not be a problem. The above four points are the preliminary measures to stabilize the situation in Sichuan. Without this, there is no way to talk about construction, and it is even more difficult to realize the Principle of People's Livelihood. Our association, based on the righteousness of respecting our homeland, presents our humble opinions and hopes that the government authorities will adopt and implement them. Those who see and sing praises will not only be our association. In a rush by telegram, we await orders. The Sichuan Native Place Association in Shanghai kowtows and stamps.

Thirteen Types of Treasury Bonds Will Be Redeemed and Paid Interest Next Month 81

Ten types of treasury bonds, including the Reissued Second-Fifth Treasury Bonds, and the Clean-Up Public Debt 7% and 6% Bonds, and the Disaster Relief Public Debt, etc., will be paid with the principal and interest due at the end of August, according to the Ministry of Finance. Bondholders can go to the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various places to pay with their bonds. The details are as follows: (1) The 44th installment of the reissued second-fifth treasury bonds, 1% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.1% of the interest will be paid; (2) The 51st installment of the 18th year customs duty treasury bonds, 0.7% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.2% of the interest will be paid; (3) The 48th installment of the 18th year demobilization treasury bonds, 0.4% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.3% of the interest will be paid; (4) The 41st installment of the 19th year cigarette treasury bonds, 1.6% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.1% of the interest will be paid; (5) The 37th installment of the 19th year customs duty treasury bonds, 0.8% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.3% of the interest will be paid; (6) The 34th installment of the 19th year rehabilitation treasury bonds, 0.6% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.4% of the interest will be paid; (7) The 32nd installment of the 20th year cigarette treasury bonds, 0.48% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.4% of the interest will be paid; (8) The 29th installment of the 20th year customs duty treasury bonds, 0.4% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.4% of the interest will be paid; (9) The 27th installment of the 20th year consolidated tax treasury bonds, 0.4% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.4% of the interest will be paid; (10) The 25th installment of the 20th year salt tax treasury bonds, 0.4% of the principal will be redeemed and 0.4% of the interest will be paid; (11) The 28th installment of the Clean-Up Public Debt 7% Bonds, 1.5% of the interest will be paid; (12) The 7th installment of the 20th year Disaster Relief Public Debt, 1.5% of the interest will be paid, the above will be paid starting from August 31; (13) The 26th installment of the Clean-Up Public Debt 6% Bonds, 1.5% of the interest will be paid, the above will be paid starting from September 1.

The Joint Office of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Fisheries Association Decides to Telegraph to Cancel the Fisheries Construction Fee 90

Since the Joint Office of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Fisheries Associations held a meeting of member representatives, the work has been extremely tense. Yesterday, another meeting of initiator representatives was held to discuss everything.

Telegraph to Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei, appealing that the association believes that Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei are using US cotton loans solely to provide relief to farmers, and should not be used for other purposes. Their concern for the people's livelihood is very deep. However, since the dispute over the collection of construction fees occurred in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang fisheries industry, it has been mediated repeatedly without resolution, causing fishermen and fish merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to suffer from the harassment and extortion of the collection office staff every day. They are in distress and have nowhere to tell. After the bankruptcy of the rural areas, it is followed by the bankruptcy of the fisheries industry. The production industry is already in a state of recession. Therefore, the meeting of initiators decided to draft a telegram to Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei, detailing the past and present situation, and immediately cancel the fisheries construction fee in order to help the people of Jiangsu. The text is about 1,000 words long. After the text is revised, it is scheduled to be sent out today or tomorrow.

The Reaction to the Rumor The Fisheries Construction Fee Collection Office announced that the collection of construction fees would be handled in accordance with the regulations and has not been slow in progress. Someone spread rumors, saying that the collection office would be canceled. After the office sent a letter to the local government to deal with the rumor-mongers in accordance with the law, Mr. Hu Diansun, the person in charge of the office, told the New News Agency reporter yesterday that since the collection office opened on April 15, due to the occurrence of collection disputes, the office has only collected once from a very small number of merchants in this city due to various reasons. The other industries have not paid. Therefore, the office has been in a state of stagnation. As for the cancellation of the collection office, it was first filed by Yu Qiaqing, a member of the Reform Association and a mediator, for the approval of the Ministry. Then, it was confirmed by the talk of Lin Kanghou, a member of the Reform Association. The office is a branch office under the Reform Committee. Then who is spreading rumors and who is spreading rumors is self-evident. The office's statement is truly what is called "cutting feet to fit shoes."

Denial of the Meng Representative Fang Junwenyin, the representative of the Shaoxing Southern Goods Industry Association in Shanghai, told the New News Agency reporter that Meng Lujiu only represents the Hangzhou Ham, Pickled Meat, and Fish Industry Association. During the mediation, he falsely claimed to represent the eight prefectures of Hangjiahu, Shaoxing, Jin, Quzhou, Yan, and Chu. Not to mention other places, as far as this office is concerned, after the Ningbo Fresh and Salted Fish Industry Association sent personnel to notify us, our association sent Yu, Zhu Zhichuan, Lei Shouchang, and Chu Zhangwei to Shanghai a few days ago to participate in the meeting of the joint office of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Fisheries Associations, declaring everything to clarify the truth.
