Shanghai Municipal Federation of Commerce Certifies Yifeng Enamel Factory as a National Goods Manufacturer 92

The National News Agency reports that the Shanghai First Special District Municipal Federation of Commerce, acting on a previous confidential report that the Yifeng Enamel Factory in this city was secretly importing enemy goods, dispatched personnel along with the Shanghai Enamel Industry Association to conduct a thorough investigation. The report indicated that since the September 18th Incident, the factory has not purchased any enemy goods. Furthermore, the Industry Association certified that the factory has, over the years, created domestic materials such as enamel powder, printing paper, crucibles, kilns, and fire bricks, which were supplied to various domestic goods manufacturers to replace enemy goods. Therefore, the factory is not only free from suspicion of being a treacherous merchant, but also effectively resists enemy goods. It is reported that the Municipal Federation of Commerce deeply admires the factory's enthusiasm for resistance and will officially certify it as a completely national goods manufacturer.

Order from the Ministry of Judicial Administration to Correct Delays in Handling Cases by the Court 93

Sufficient Preparation Required Before Court Sessions, Skillful Questioning Especially Important During Hearings. Yesterday, the Shanghai Local Court received an order, No. 1471, from the Jiangsu Higher Court, which was forwarded from the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The order stated that while judges should focus and question skillfully during court hearings, sufficient preparation before the hearings is even more crucial to avoid aimless questioning. Recent investigations have found that many judges do not thoroughly review case files or determine a direction for investigation beforehand. As a result, initial court sessions often follow routine procedures without grasping the key points, requiring at least one additional session per case. This not only hinders the proper administration of justice but also wastes time. The cumulative effect over a year is significant and causes delays, potentially leading to collusion and alteration of evidence, thereby obscuring the truth of the case. The presiding officers of the respective courts bear supervisory responsibility. Hereafter, they must strictly correct the handling of cases by the investigators, prosecutors, and judges to achieve greater efficiency and effectiveness, while also saving personnel and expenses. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued to the court and forwarded to its subordinates for unified attention and compliance.

Arabic Numerals for Number Codes

Telegraph Bureau to Implement Order Tomorrow 97

To facilitate the public, the Ministry of Communications previously decided to use Arabic numerals to replace house numbers and other numerical figures in telegrams. For example, the number 1312 or 1312 yuan can be written as (1312) and calculated as one telegraphic word, but it must be enclosed in parentheses to avoid confusion. However, if there are more than four digits, starting from five digits, it will be calculated as two words, and so on. The Ministry of Communications has formally ordered the local Ministry of Communications Telegraph Bureau to comply with this measure, which will be implemented starting August 1st. However, this measure only applies to domestic telegrams and does not apply to Nanyang (Southeast Asia) and European and American countries.

Meeting Between Marine Engineers of Misao Company and Management to Discuss Pay Raise Conditions 99

Recently, the Misao Shipping Company announced the cancellation of year-end bonuses and the change to monthly salary increases, which aroused opposition from the marine engineers. The treatment of the officers and engineers is different (captains, chief mates, and second mates are officers, while chief engineers, first assistant engineers, second assistant engineers, and third assistant engineers are engineers). The engineers rose up in opposition. Yesterday, the company sent Li Yuncheng to the marine engineers' association to negotiate with Feng Yuming, Mao Jinsheng, Huang Yucai, and others. The company representative decided on the following salary increase plan: For the new Misao ships, the chief engineer will receive an additional 25 yuan, the first assistant engineer 15 yuan, the second assistant engineer 10 yuan, and the third assistant engineer 5 yuan. For the Misao ships, the chief engineer will receive an additional 10 yuan, the first assistant engineer 10 yuan, and the second assistant engineer 10 yuan. For the Misao Jing ships, the chief engineer will receive an additional 10 yuan, the first assistant engineer 10 yuan, and the second assistant engineer 10 yuan. However, the marine engineers' association insisted that the increases must be implemented according to the following plan: For the new Misao ships, the captain should receive an additional 75 yuan per month, the chief engineer 50 yuan, the chief mate and first assistant engineer 25 yuan each, the second mate and second assistant engineer 15 yuan each, and the third mate and third assistant engineer 10 yuan each. For the Misao ships, the captain should receive an additional 50 yuan, the chief engineer 20 yuan, and the chief mate and first assistant engineer 15 yuan each, and the second mate and second assistant engineer 10 yuan each. For the Misao Jing ships, the captain should receive an additional 50 yuan, the chief engineer 20 yuan, the chief mate 25 yuan, the first assistant engineer 20 yuan, and the second mate and second assistant engineer 15 yuan each. The company representative agreed to consult with superiors and respond later.

Report on the Tragic Situation of Banditry in Henan 100

Jisheng Society Appeals for Relief Funds. The China Jisheng Society recently received a telegram from Guo Jundai, the Administrative Inspector of the Ninth District of Henan, stating that the Southern Henan Special Zone, including the old counties of Huangchuan, Guangshan, Xixian, Shangcheng, Gushi, Luoshan, and Xinyang, and the new counties of Jingfu and Lihuang, were once known for their prosperity. However, since the spread of communist doctrines from Wuhan, which soon reached Huangma in Hubei, the people of Southern Henan feared its harm to society. In the summer of the 16th year of the Republic (1927), they gathered tens of thousands of people to advance on Macheng. Although they were unable to completely eradicate the bandits due to limited strength, this demonstration prevented the bandits from stepping into Southern Henan for two years. Later, the country faced many misfortunes, and internal wars occurred frequently. Taking advantage of the opportunity, starting from May of the 18th year of the Republic (1929), a group of only dozens of people with more than thirty guns launched an uprising. They exploited the wavering youths, bribed poor farmers with small benefits, and used vagrants as vanguards to wreak havoc everywhere. As a result, Shangcheng fell, followed by Gushi, and Guangshan and Luoshan were subsequently lost, with Yichuan also in imminent danger. Only Xixian remained unaffected. However, the bandits responded like an echo, and the disaster was equally severe. Last year, the army achieved victory and established the two counties of Jingfu and Lihuang in succession, and the area was gradually pacified. However, the remnants unfortunately remained hidden in the border areas and showed signs of resurgence. In addition to harming the people through robbery, murder, and looting, there were also so-called "Skinning Pavilion," "Mass Graves," and "Exposed Bone Piles," whose cruelty was so severe that even heaven, earth, and ghosts would weep. Furthermore, countless others fled or died of starvation or disease. Statistics show that the original population of over three million has been reduced to only five or six tenths, and many of those remaining are barely alive. The organizations of rural villages and markets have been completely destroyed and reduced to ruins. In addition, famine and pestilence are converging, creating a scene of utter desolation. There is not a single piece of clean land, and no household has a single grain of overnight food. Some abandon their parents because they cannot provide even thin gruel, and some abandon their wives and children because they cannot even get their fill of vegetable roots. Alas, the survivors cannot live through the day. It is earnestly hoped that you will show great compassion and provide generous relief. The report requesting relief has arrived. Previously, the Society sent relief workers to Lihuang, Jingfu, and other counties to investigate the situation, which was indescribable. The reported situation was even less severe than what was witnessed firsthand. Where can we find large amounts of relief funds to help these millions of survivors on the verge of starvation?

Lü Gongwang Raises the Issue of Military Jurisdiction After Being Accused 101

Lü Gongwang, also known as Dai Zhi, formerly the Acting Military Governor of Zhejiang and Garrison Commander of Jiahu, has recently been engaged in business in Shanghai. On February 23rd of this year, he pledged 100 bales of Sanyang brand cotton yarn from the Yongyuheji Textile Company, which he managed, to the Sanma Road Silk Industry Bank for a loan of 9,000 taels of silver. When the loan matured and he failed to redeem the pledge, the creditor was unable to retrieve the goods from the warehouse. The guarantor, Dai Zibin, director of the Kailuan Coal Mine Business Department, refused to handle the matter. Therefore, Luo Qinghua, manager of the Silk Industry Bank, hired Dong Yu as a lawyer and filed a lawsuit with the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, accusing Lü and Dai of joint fraud. The details of the interrogation have been reported previously. On the morning before yesterday, Judge Wu Fanglian summoned both parties for a continued hearing in Criminal Court No. 2. According to the defendant Lü Dai Zhi, he is currently a staff officer in the 55th Division of the Army (Commander Wu Sui) and is an active-duty soldier. According to Article 10 of the Army Trial Law, soldiers should be tried by military law, and ordinary courts cannot accept the case. He requested that the case be transferred to a military court for trial. The lawyer representing the plaintiff stated that the defendant Lü Dai Zhi is indeed a formal businessman and did not raise the issue of military status during the previous hearing. He is only raising it today, which clearly shows that he has indeed committed a crime and is trying to evade responsibility. He is raising the issue of military status to deceive the court and should be noted. Mr. Pan from the Bank of China was summoned to court. Because the defendant raised the issue of military jurisdiction, he was not questioned. The judge adjourned the hearing to August 4th to verify the information before proceeding.

Settlement of the Lawsuit Involving the Qing Dyeing Guild in the Beijing Style 103

The Qing Dyeing Guild in the Beijing Style, located on Fuyou Road in the city, had over a thousand dyeing workers during its heyday. The guild was also quite prosperous and owned real estate on Carter Road. Later, with the influx of foreign goods, the Beijing-style Qing dyeing industry declined sharply. All dyeing workers gradually lost their jobs. The strong changed professions, while the old and weak simply sat and waited for death. There were two to three hundred people. Moreover, the guild was heavily in debt. Later, because it was unable to maintain the livelihood of these unemployed workers, directors Li Chuanyao and Feng Liangfu convened a meeting of all directors and decided to sell the guild's assets to repay debts and distribute the remaining funds to the unemployed workers for alternative livelihoods. At that time, it was also resolved to sell the Immortal Weng Temple in the Fuyou Road Guild. However, the tenants renting the houses in the guild were ordered to move out. Unexpectedly, Zhang Jiacai and Li Shengxian, who were also in the dyeing industry, gathered their colleagues and advocated for the preservation of the guild's assets. They sued Li Chuanyao and others for selling public property in the judicial office. The lawsuit has been ongoing since February of the 17th year of the Republic (1928), totaling five years, and has now reached a conclusion. The verdict was in favor of Li Chuanyao and others. Therefore, the tenant representatives Wang Jingru and Zhang Jiacai were repeatedly urged to move out of the guild's premises immediately, or they would be demolished. However, the tenant representatives Wang Jingru and Zhang Jiacai were in a dilemma because they were entrusted by the preservation faction. They submitted a petition to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting that the Qing Dyeing Guild representative Li Chuanyao be ordered to postpone the demolition. The Municipal Public Security Bureau found that in this case, Li Chuanyao and others had already won the final verdict and should be handled in accordance with Articles 10 and 23 of the Tenant Lease Rules. Yesterday, the local Section One Branch of the Second District was specially ordered to summon representatives from both sides to provide proper guidance. Chief Shen summoned guild representative Li Chuanyao and Feng Liangfu, tenant representatives Wang Jingru and Zhang Jiacai, and preservationists Li Shengxian and Zhang Jiacai to the office at 3:00 PM yesterday. Under benevolent persuasion, tenant representatives Wang Jingru and others were willing to vacate the premises within twenty days and provided a written guarantee. Li Chuanyao and others were instructed not to demolish the houses within the time limit, and Zhang Jiacai and others were not allowed to obstruct them again. The years-long lawsuit was thus concluded.

Page 12

Municipal Zoo to Open on August 1st 108

In addition to existing animals, special purchases of elephants, apes, lions, and tigers will be made from Siam. The Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road in the South City, constructed for one year, is now complete and ready to open on August 1st.

Construction Process 109

The zoo is located across from the Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road, the original site of the Qinpu. Construction began in August of last year and was divided into three phases. The first phase was completed in December of last year, and the second phase was completed in February of this year. The Municipal Engineering Bureau handed over each phase to the Municipal Government, which dispatched personnel along with the Municipal Education Bureau to accept them. The Municipal Education Bureau then dispatched personnel to take custody of them. Before the opening, Shen Xiangrui, former director of the First Public School Garden, was responsible for managing the animals.

Opening Tomorrow 110

According to the zoo's original plan, it was originally intended to open this spring. Initially, the zoo's construction funds were allocated from the Music Hall's construction funds, with 20,000 yuan allocated from the Music Hall construction fees and 7,000 yuan for purchasing animals, and 13,000 yuan for the cost of construction. Later, due to the construction of the peacock pavilion and miscellaneous poultry houses, the budget was exceeded and the Municipal Government was asked for further funds. The project was completed in May. It could have opened in June, but the Examination Committee borrowed the park for office space, so the opening was delayed until August 1st. The opening rules have been announced by the Municipal Education Bureau. Tickets are six copper coins per person, half price for children, and annual passes are one silver yuan each, all sold at the zoo's ticket office.

Purchasing Animals 111

The zoo currently has more than fifty kinds of animals, the most expensive being a pair of lions at 2,150 yuan, a tiger at 950 yuan, and a leopard at 210 yuan, all purchased from Nanyang last year. The total amount of consumption by all animals is about 10 yuan per day, especially lions, tigers, and leopards, which consume the most, eating about 7 yuan of beef per day. Currently, in addition to purchasing unique animals at any time, it is planned to purchase elephants, apes, and other animals from Siam. An elephant is currently being negotiated, costing about 2,000 yuan.

Director Appointed 112

The director of the zoo has been internally determined to be Shen Xiangrui, the former director of the First Municipal Public School Garden. The official appointment will be announced by the Municipal Education Bureau today. The internal staff have not yet been announced. The Education Bureau also intends to contact the Municipal Health Bureau to select a veterinarian as a consultant for the zoo.

After the four men got into the car, they drove to the corner of Route Vallon in the French Concession and stopped. One person remained in the car, and after the other three got out of the car, two robbers broke into the Shunchang Tobacco and Paper Shop, owned by Chen Shunyi, a local, at No. 32 along the road, and committed robbery. One robber stood guard outside the door. They robbed more than seventy yuan in banknotes. After the robbery, the robbers got into the car and ordered the driver to drive to the Yuyongchang Tobacco and Paper Shop at No. 12 Shanzhong Road, where they robbed more than three hundred yuan in banknotes. Afterwards, they stopped briefly on Route Pichon in the French Concession. One of the robbers remained in the car to guard it. At 12:45 PM, they ordered the driver to drive back to the automobile company. On the way, they passed near the Duoyi Restaurant on Route Edward VII and ordered the car to stop. They then pulled out a gun to intimidate the driver. After the robbers got out of the car, they fled into the small alley next to the east side of the restaurant. When the car stopped on Route Pichon, passersby noticed that it was suspicious and reported the car's license number to the Songshan Road Patrol Room. At this time, the two tobacco and paper shop owners who were robbed reported the robbery to the patrol room. The Western patrol chief immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. At 1:30 PM, they went to the Huifang Automobile Company and brought back the car used in the robbery and the suspect driver Huang Xinpu to the patrol room for custody and interrogation. This morning, they were sent to the Second Special District Court for handling.

Ministry of Communications Issues Order on Principles for Entrusting Long-Distance Telephone Services to Three Telecommunications Bureaus 117

| To avoid past competition between national and provincial operations | In light of the increasing development of provincial long-distance telephone services in recent years, the Ministry of Communications, considering that, according to telecommunications regulations, the ministry should be in charge of operations, believes that independent setups would not only violate regulations and disrupt the system but also make unified management impossible, leading to operational competition. Therefore, the ministry has drafted fourteen principles for entrusting provincial governments to manage long-distance telephone services on behalf of the ministry in order to achieve cooperation between the ministry and provinces and jointly promote the rapid development of telecommunications, thereby avoiding past competition between national and provincial operations. These principles have been approved by the Executive Yuan, and the ministry issued an order to its subordinate Telephone Bureau, Telegraph Bureau, and Telecommunications Bureau yesterday to implement them.

The full text of the principles is also promulgated and recorded below:

(1) The Ministry of Communications may, without prejudice to the scope of its own telegraph and telephone services, entrust provincial governments to manage long-distance telephone services (hereinafter referred to as "entrusted long-distance telephone services") on behalf of the ministry, based on actual needs. The scope of such long-distance telephone services shall be limited to the boundaries of the province. (2) Before laying out entrusted long-distance telephone services, a project proposal shall be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval. The project proposal shall clearly state the following items and include detailed diagrams: (A) Total length of the entire line, (B) Planned locations for telephone calls along the line, (C) Distance between each telephone location, (D) Line construction plan, (E) Equipment manufacturing plan, (F) Telephone connection method, (G) Estimated construction period for line laying and equipment installation, (H) Project budget, (I) Overview of operations. (3) For long-distance telephone services that have already been established by provinces, the provincial governments shall complete the procedures in accordance with Article 2 and submit them to the Ministry of Communications for approval. If the Ministry of Communications deems any aspect to be non-compliant, it may consult and modify the proposal. (4) The construction of entrusted long-distance telephone services shall be carried out in accordance with the plans and regulations approved by the Ministry of Communications. The Ministry of Communications may also send personnel to supervise all aspects of the work at any time. (5) The tariffs and all operational methods for entrusted long-distance telephone services shall be approved by the Ministry of Communications. (6) A certain percentage of the total operating revenue of entrusted long-distance telephone services shall be turned over to the Ministry of Communications. The specific amount shall be determined by the ministry and the province through separate consultations based on the operating revenue situation. (7) The operating status of entrusted long-distance telephone services shall be reported to the Ministry of Communications for review in detail on a regular basis. (8) The Ministry of Communications may borrow entrusted long-distance telephone lines for transmitting telegrams, but only to the extent that it does not affect the original telephone utility. (9) Inter-provincial telephone calls shall not be entrusted to provincial governments to manage on behalf of the ministry. If provinces have already interconnected for telephone calls, the Ministry of Communications may acquire them for management at a price or temporarily rent their utility poles. (10) The Ministry of Communications, if deemed necessary, may take over the entrusted long-distance telephone services for management. All lines, machinery, houses, equipment, and other items shall be estimated at depreciated current prices. (11) The lines of entrusted long-distance telephone services shall avoid being installed parallel to the lines of the ministry's long-distance telephone services. If this situation already exists, another solution shall be devised. (12) In places where the Ministry of Communications has telegraph bureaus or radio stations, entrusted long-distance telephone services shall not engage in disguised telegram services such as notification calls or telephone transmission of telegrams. (13) When provincial governments need to establish military long-distance telephone services, they must first consult the Ministry of Military Affairs, which shall then forward the consultation to the Ministry of Communications for record. Upon the completion of military affairs, the facilities shall be transferred to the management of the Ministry of Communications. (14) These principles shall be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation for implementation.

Reorganization of the Board of Directors of the Municipal Martial Arts Hall 118

Wu Tiecheng, the director of the Municipal Martial Arts Hall, recognizing the importance of martial arts in physical education and tactics, decided to expand the organization of the hall and make it popular throughout the city. Furthermore, due to the resignations, departures from Shanghai, and deaths of many board members since the January 28th Incident, there are many vacancies. In order to fill these vacancies and ensure the health of the board of directors, it was decided to reorganize the board. Therefore, at 7 p.m. the night before last, a meeting was held at the French Concession YMCA, specially entrusting Li Dachao, the section chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government, to discuss the reorganization of the hall's affairs in conjunction with hall directors Ye Liang, Li Zunguang, Chen Xuliang, Gu Wensheng, and Ling Weichuan. Li Dachao presided over the meeting, and Qian Weiju recorded the minutes. (2) Regarding the selection of directors, it was resolved that they must possess the following four qualifications: (1) prominent figures in society, (2) martial arts experts, (3) martial arts enthusiasts, and (4) those with close ties to the hall. The allocation of these positions shall be as follows: 20 persons shall be introduced by the winding-up committee of the standing committee of the hall and presented to the mayor for approval and appointment, and the remaining 25 persons shall be directly appointed by the mayor. (3) Regarding the maintenance of the hall's affairs during the transitional period, it was resolved that the daily maintenance of the hall's affairs before the new board of directors is formed shall be handled by the winding-up committee in conjunction with Section Chief Li. (4) Regarding the handover, it was resolved that it shall be handled jointly with Section Chief Li after the new board of directors is formed.

China Relief Association Prepares to Organize Common People's Domestic Goods Sales Teams 119

Please factories give support. The China Relief Association has been sparing no effort in engaging in domestic relief work for many years. Recently, in view of the rising cost of living and the large number of unemployed people who have come to request relief, often several times a day, it is planned to organize common people's domestic goods sales teams to reduce the number of beggars in society and prevent the breeding of thieves. The goods sold will be limited to daily necessities, and the profits earned each day will be distributed equally among the members of each sales team to ensure a livelihood. It has now been decided to start with ten teams, each with five people, with a head of the team to guide the team. Anyone with a clean background, regardless of gender, who is unable to make a living and can provide a guarantor, can register at the Relief Section of the association on Longmen Road, Racecourse Road, for assignment. It would be greatly appreciated if domestic goods factories could entrust the association to help promote sales or show compassion for the hungry and drowning and generously donate to the cause.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Second Branch of the High Court to Request Exemption of Flower and Tree Nursery Land 120

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday wrote to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court to request the exemption of the land of Xu Wenyuan, a flower and tree nursery operator. The original letter stated: "We hereby notify you that on the 28th of this month, we received a letter from the Flower and Tree Nursery Association stating that the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court is constructing a new prison in the Pusong District and intends to requisition the land of member Xu Wenyuan. We have found that Xu Wenyuan is located in Block 7 of the 30th Bao, an area with high and airy terrain, suitable soil, and access to waterways. He has devoted years of effort to afforestation and soil cultivation, collecting tens of thousands of seedlings of rare and exotic trees, planting them by hand, and establishing their roots. The branches and stems are still weak and difficult to transplant. If they are abandoned, they will have no chance of survival. Even with compensation, it would be impossible to compensate for even a fraction of the loss. Moreover, according to the shape of the land being requisitioned for the new prison, viewing the entire area, our member's nursery is located at the tip of a corner and not in the center, making avoidance highly possible. Furthermore, the land being requisitioned is already more than 160 mu. Reducing the area by more than 10 mu would not seem to hinder the overall plan for the construction of the new prison. The layout of the new prison, the number of buildings, etc., are arrangements for the future. The construction can be carried out according to the size of the land. If there is not enough land, other open spaces can still be requisitioned. Even if the security perimeter is affected, a river can be opened to compensate. Why is it necessary to destroy a nursery that has been cultivated for many years? Tree seedlings are not comparable to potted flowers, which can be sold at any time. At least ten years are needed for a tree to mature and become profitable. Now, the seedlings have been cultivated for several years, and once they are forced to relocate, they will become waste. Moreover, the same land has differences in height and suitability of soil, and the timing is even more important. Given these difficulties, relocation is truly difficult and must be requested to be exempted from requisition in order to maintain a livelihood. Please forward our request to the Second Branch for approval." We have found that nurseries are different from farmland. Once relocated, the weak branches and stems of the seedlings are very difficult to transplant and will inevitably be abandoned. If their livelihoods are destroyed in this way, how can they survive? Moreover, according to the map, Xu Wenyuan's nursery being requisitioned is located at the very tip of a corner, and the land area is only one-tenth of the total area being requisitioned, making avoidance possible. It does not seem to hinder the overall prison plan. Accordingly, we are writing to your branch to explain the situation and earnestly request that you consider the difficulty of relocating the nursery and exempt Xu Wenyuan's nursery from requisition. If the area does not meet the original plan, please requisition other open spaces to make up the difference, so that both prison administration and people's livelihood can be taken into account. We believe this is in the spirit of public interest.

Criminal Investigations Must Not Extend Detention Periods 122

Follow rules and bring to speedy conclusion. The Shanghai District Court Procuratorate yesterday received Instruction No. 2263 from the Jiangsu High Court Procuratorate, which forwarded it from the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The instruction stated that the investigation period and rules for criminal trials are strictly regulated, and the period of detention of the accused is clearly stipulated in the Criminal Procedure Law. When a procurator receives a case, they should bring it to a speedy conclusion and must not arbitrarily delay it simply because the time limit has not expired. However, in recent times, procurators have often been negligent and perfunctory in handling cases, failing to conduct thorough investigations. When the investigation period expires, they often try to cover up their mistakes. When the accused's detention period expires, they use the legal provisions for extending detention and apply for an extension. Eventually, when no further extensions are possible, they hastily file a lawsuit in an attempt to shirk responsibility. This is completely unacceptable. Therefore, you are hereby ordered to instruct your subordinates that when handling cases in the future, they must conduct speedy investigations and bring them to a conclusion in accordance with the law. If the above-mentioned situation is found again, strict punishment will be imposed and no leniency will be shown. This order is hereby issued. Upon receiving this order, you are hereby ordered to instruct your subordinates to comply.

Shanghai Native Yellow Wine Trade Association Convened a Members' Meeting Yesterday 123

Three new tax countermeasure proposals are resolved. The Shanghai Native Yellow Wine Trade Association held its second members' representative meeting at 11 a.m. yesterday. Twenty-six representatives attended the meeting. Zhang Dafu, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yuan Hongjun, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Zhang Dalian, representative of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Wine Industry Federation, attended. Fang Zhongheng, the chairman, was ill, so Han Xingwei was elected as the temporary chairman. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, the discussion focused on how to request improvements to the new tax regulations, which are mostly detrimental to the industry, in order to seek relief. After public deliberation, the following three measures were resolved: (1) The provisions of the new tax that are detrimental to the industry should be amended. (2) Special stamps should still be retained. (3) The quantity of containers should be converted to the market scale according to the original jin. If these objectives cannot be achieved, all workshops will stop operations and brewing. The trade association will send a letter to the Shanghai Soy Sauce and Pickles Trade Association, notifying its members to stop taking and transporting consignment goods. At the same time, a detailed explanation will be sent to the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Wine Industry Federation to argue the case. A circular will also be sent to the Wine-Making Workers' Union, asking them to inform the original workers of the factories to stop working and find other livelihoods. A letter will also be presented to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, asking them to uphold justice and provide assistance. We vow not to achieve our goals and are willing to sacrifice our business in order to achieve final victory. The entire resolution was passed. The meeting adjourned at 1 p.m.

Suspicious Sudden Death of an Employee at Zhengfeng Clothing Store 135

Fresh blood flowed from the lower body; sent to the District Court for autopsy. Zhengfeng Clothing Store, located at No. 274, Gonghe Xin Road, Zhabei, was established with funds raised by Nanxun merchants. Its manager, Han Guisheng, 46, is from Nanxun. The store had just begun operations in early March of this year. Han had a friend from the same hometown, Gu Suizhi, 31 years old. Considering that Gu had been unemployed for a long time, Han introduced him to the clothing store as an employee. Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, Gu suddenly suffered from a severe ailment, exhibiting alarming symptoms. He became speechless, unresponsive, and lost consciousness. Upon seeing this, Han quickly hired a vehicle to rush Gu to the Red Cross Epidemic Hospital on Xinmin Road, Zhabei, for emergency treatment. However, Gu died en route to the hospital. The hospital, following procedure, did not register the death and sent the body to the mortuary. However, the hospital doctor discovered that fresh blood was flowing incessantly from Gu's blue cloth trousers around the lower body. Suspecting something amiss, the hospital questioned Han, who claimed that the deceased had suffered from ringworm and other skin conditions in the scrotum area before. He had sought treatment at the Lianyi Charity Association in Hanqiao some days prior, where a doctor diagnosed it as a result of syphilis, leading Gu to discontinue treatment. Gu then became delusional, believing that the ailment was caused by evil spirits and privately sought treatment from a female shaman without success. The previous evening, Gu had washed the area with alum water, and the bleeding may have been caused by abrasion. Upon learning this information, the hospital doctor, suspecting other circumstances, notified the Fourth District Public Security Bureau. District Chief Lai dispatched personnel to investigate and instructed Lu Abaobao, the head of the Eleventh Baojia (neighborhood watch unit), to petition the Shanghai District Court for an autopsy. Around 4:00 PM yesterday, a prosecutor, accompanied by forensic officials, arrived at the hospital morgue to conduct a detailed examination. However, a death certificate was not completed at the time; the Baojia chief was only instructed to arrange for the burial of the body.

Autopsy Results of the Deceased Coachman 142

Injured Ribs Led to Fatal Spleen Injury; Suspect Liang Yutao Sentenced to Four Years in Prison.

Jiang Yuqing, a 37-year-old from Yangzhou, employed as a driver at the Fada Coach Company at No. 191, O'Ka Road, got into a dispute on the afternoon of this month with Liang Yutao, a competitor from No. 189 next door, over business competition. The police immediately dispatched detective Liu Shuxun to re-arrest Liang Yutao and escort him to the First Special District Court. Liang denied injuring Jiang Yuqing's waist with his fists. The court sent a prosecutor to examine the deceased Jiang Yuqing's injuries, but the true cause of death remained unclear. Later, a forensic examination revealed that two ribs had been fractured, causing fatal damage to the spleen. Yesterday, a judge presided over the Third Criminal Court for interrogation. Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the police station presented the previous circumstances, stating that a Japanese constable was present to testify about the arrest. Constable No. 223 stated that he saw a crowd gathered at the scene and witnessed two Chinese men fighting, so he arrested them both. The defendant firmly denied the charges. After the forensic report was read aloud in court, and after arguments from the police attorney and the defendant's attorney, Liang Yutao was sentenced to four years in prison as a warning. The number of days of pre-trial detention was to be deducted from the prison sentence at a rate of two days credited for each day served.

Chunqiu Yaguang

The New Red Peril Wings 149

After reading Xianxian's article "Red Pills," I also have a few words to say. In fact, this thing is spreading too widely. Not only in Shanghai, but almost the whole country has a trend of being engulfed by the red behemoth, which can be called "the new red peril!" Its speed of spread and the intensity of the disaster have surpassed the Communist Party. The Communists only ravaged the land of several provinces, and the damage was to the lives and property of a portion of the people; the new red peril is like mercury seeping into the ground, penetrating everywhere, not limited to one corner, and sufficient to shackle the entire nation. Moreover, the Communists can still be suppressed by military force, but once the new red peril has spread, it is not easy to find a fundamental way to ban it; the inability to ban opium is a precedent!

In fact, the disaster of opium cannot be compared with the new red peril. To ban opium is not an impossible task. As everyone knows, opium is the juice of the poppy, and the poppy must be planted, and it must take a considerable amount of time to bear fruit, which cannot be done secretly by individuals. But red pills can be manufactured in a small room to supply a large number of consumers. There were not many places where poppies were planted in the past. Now even Jiangsu has planted them. If the planters are strictly banned and the import of foreign opium is strictly prohibited at the same time, it is not impossible to ban it. Only red pills can be secretly manufactured anytime and anywhere, and can be manufactured in large quantities; even if they are seized, another secret manufacturing organization can be set up; unlike opium, which is not produced in most local areas and must be transported from other places, the rapid spread of red pills is also a major reason.

Smoking opium is aristocratic. At present, if your pocket is not two-eighths full, don't even think about lying on a couch, as Xianxian said. I don't think so. Smoking red pills also requires two-eighths full. In fact, there are more people smoking red pills than smoking opium, but the cost of red pills often exceeds that of opium. Or maybe it should be said that the equipment for smoking opium must be exquisite, and at the very least, you must have a good opium pipe. When smoking, you must carefully load the bowl, and after one bowl is finished, you must put down the pipe and carefully load the second bowl. It is not as simple and quick as smoking red pills, which does not require loading bowl by bowl, and can consume dozens of pills in one breath. The reason why laborers (such as rickshaw pullers) abandon opium and take pills is mostly for convenience and speed. There is also another level: if the smoker cooks the opium himself, he must buy raw opium for a lot of money and slowly cook it into smoke. Red pills can be bought at any time for eight cents, and can be smoked as soon as they are purchased. Therefore, most of those who smoke opium are leisure classes and intellectuals, so it naturally looks like it has become aristocratic. However, it cannot be judged by the amount of consumption. There are also people who smoke red pills for a few yuan a day. Now many places ban pills but not opium, which further illustrates that the harm of the new red peril is greater than that of opium.

Sweat Lanxi 150

Sweat is a special product of summer. It is also produced by hard work; and also by excessive entertainment.

People in the leisure class and the property class have fewer opportunities to sweat. They, or she, drink ice under the activity of electric fans and between the surrounding air conditioning pipes to feel the heat. They are unlikely to sweat much. If there is any, it is just a few drops on the tip of the nose, which is not only not stinky, but also, it is said, fragrant丨丨and especially young ladies and wives, because they are covered with the best imported talcum powder, which emits a kind of fragrance in secret. If they sweat a little more, then the powder applied to their bodies dissolves with the sweat, and a chemical reaction produces a charming fragrance, which has never been disliked by gentlemen and all noble men. This kind of sweat should be given considerable praise and allowed to exist.

However, turning to another point, there is a kind of stinky sweat that makes you want to vomit for three days, which you dare not accept but often have to accept, and that is the sweat of coolies.

The small workers and rickshaw pullers who are constantly evaporating under the hot sun and wearing coarse cloth clothes have no time to take a bath at all, so they sweat dozens of times a day, and they can only let it get wet and dry, and then dry and wet again, repeating this cycle, day after day, (they either don't know what hygiene is, or they don't have many clothes to change, so each piece of clothing is worn for many days,) which will refine a kind of acidic, extraordinarily bad smell. No wonder the modern young ladies twisting on the road often cover their jade noses with a small handkerchief, and also lock their eyebrows that have been dyed, showing a contemptuous attitude.

Our enjoyment is far less comfortable than the rich, but also less laborious than the coolies. We often sweat, and when we taste it ourselves, we don't feel it's stinky, but think it's fragrant. However, this is a biased and subjective judgment. In fact, we, these so-called "stinky men," where is there any fragrance?

Sweat is a special product of summer. It is fragrant when it comes out on young ladies, but it becomes stinky when it comes out on coolies. However, "sweat" does not know this, but it has to come out on the coolies, alas, God knows.

Bu Zhao Zhixian 151

Seeing the advertisement for the 500,000 yuan lottery prize in the newspaper, my heart couldn't help but flutter a little. Really, this "500,000" is such a large number! Hearing it is enough to make people envious, and if you ever win it, the joy is needless to say. All the so-called difficult problems can be solved easily... Looking at the newspaper, I was thinking blankly.

"How to spend this 500,000 yuan?" This question began to annoy me, for fear that kidnappers would take the opportunity, and robbers would come to the door.

Actively thinking: Let's use this money to start a business! But it seems that there are too many businesses to start at present. This has to be started, and that has to be done. At first glance, the number of 500,000 is quite a lot, but to do this and that, it feels small and not enough!

Passively thinking: Let's use it to help a group of poor relatives and friends, and do some charity work, but I feel that there are too many poor relatives and friends to count. This one has to be helped, and that one has to be saved! The same goes for charitable organizations. This 500,000 yuan is still not enough!

The first is not enough, the second is not enough, the third is still not enough!

"How to spend this 500,000 yuan?" This question began to annoy me.

Benefactor of Charity - Master of Chun Yu Lou 152

The thermometer is quickly rising to 100 degrees; people are enveloped in heat, and dogs are also panting with their tongues out. Ordinary poor people are still struggling to earn a living, with sweat dripping like rain. Although they constantly complain about the heat, what good does it do?

Therefore, charitable people are providing tea and dispensing cooling medicine... continuously offering practical benefits to the impoverished, who are truly benefiting greatly.

But isn't that so? Often, a coolie, feeling the heat, seeks some relief from those dispensing medicine, but their servants often bully and scold, giving them the cold shoulder unless you have a personal relationship with them. Otherwise, they will take the entire batch home to give to relatives. This is not just an individual occurrence, but also happens with organized groups providing aid. Indeed, the donors are kept in the dark and unaware.

If you don't believe it, just look at disaster relief efforts and donations. Many, many people fill their private pockets! Under the guise of offering assistance and the name of fundraising, they boldly engage in despicable acts, causing donors to lose heart.

I personally saw a coolie being scolded for asking a charitable organization for a bottle of cooling medicine, while they were taking entire boxes of it home. Therefore, I specifically wrote this article, hoping that charitable people will investigate whether their servants are doing such things!

Zhang Henshui, Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

Poor and Lowly Sufferings, Sick Soldiers Fall Behind, Sacrificing Sweetly to Return Home, Sentimental Soldiers.

Sheng Shimin, looking at her, thought she resembled a young lady and asked, "Miss, is this Commander Zhao's house?" Lipstick Application Tips 154

If you apply a thick layer of lipstick heavily on your lips when putting on makeup, your lips will tend to become hard.

If your lips have already become hard, don't be discouraged. Simply apply glycerin and lemon to make them soft and enhance their beautiful color, achieving the standard of being both red and vibrant.

If the lipstick you are using is dry and doesn't seem to have any oil in it, apply some moisturizing cream to your lips before applying the lipstick. (Moisturizing cream refers to ordinary vanishing cream, white jade cream, Hazelnut cream, etc.)

If your lips are thick, it's best not to apply lipstick all the way to the edges of your lips. Be sure not to apply it there. If your lips are thin, then apply it completely, even if it goes beyond the lip line.

After applying lipstick, it's best to wipe off some of the color slightly. It's important to know that ordinary mirrors, especially blurry, uneven, or inferior mirrors, often reflect an image that is thinner and darker than reality.

The most scientific and artistic way to apply lipstick is not what most modern girls imagine. It's commonly thought that the most appropriate and convenient method is to apply it horizontally, from the left end of the lips to the right end, and then from the right end to the left end. In fact, this is not the best method. It should be changed to a vertical application, from the upper lip to the lower lip, and then from the lower lip to the upper lip, because the skin in this area also grows from top to bottom and from bottom to top. At the same time, apply it along the lines of the lips. This method takes more time, but you will be immediately satisfied after applying it. If you don't believe it, please try it right away. (Pei Mo)

Sock-Wearing Tips 155

There is nothing more annoying and frustrating than having a hole in your sock. It is absolutely true that a hole in a sock is very unsightly. The fact is that the amount of time spent on carefully putting on socks should be several times more than the time we usually spend paying attention to them. Socks that don't fit properly, are the wrong size, or are out of style often make us annoyed with our socks, which is really troublesome. For example, sock sizes, styles, and brands vary. Some sock manufacturers often make them half a size larger or smaller than what we normally wear. There is nothing more unsightly and annoying than socks that are wrinkled and not straight on the ankles and knees, or sock tops that are crooked and patterns that are skewed. On the other hand, there is nothing more unsightly and annoying than having holes in the heel and toe areas of new socks. It's also very embarrassing to wear socks that are snagged and unravelling.

If socks have patterns, a straight seam down the back, or a pointed heel design, extra care should be taken to ensure they are straight, neat, and tight. To achieve these three conditions, first choose socks that are the right size and style, and then use garters to hold them up. A single elastic band will never be satisfactory.

As for what color and style of socks to wear, it cannot be generalized. You can wear whatever you like, but the weather and season should be considered. For example, in the summer, you should wear silk or gauze socks in light colors such as white, light yellow, or lotus root pink. If you are sensitive to the cold, then in the winter, you should give up thin silk stockings, which are only good-looking and not warm, and wear thick and warm wool socks. Otherwise, you will suffer from frostbite.

Finally, let's talk about sock-wearing superstitions. We occasionally accidentally wear a sock inside out, which is considered very unlucky. However, English girls think differently. They consider it very lucky to find their socks inside out. If the inside-out sock is on the left foot, it's especially lucky. There is also another wonderful superstition: when wearing a new pair of socks for the first time, if you sleep with the sock worn on your right foot during the day under your pillow, the dream you have that night will definitely come true. If you have a nightmare, that's terrible. (Pei)

(Paris, 30th Reuters) On the final day of the Davis Cup tournament, French Kohlen Schreiber defeated England's Austin by three to two, with scores of 5-7, 6-4, 4-6, 6-4, 6-4. France tied the score at two-two. The final outcome depends on the battle between Panry (England) and Merlin (France). England is considered to have a good chance.

(Havas Agency, Paris, 29th) The England-France Davis Cup tournament, on the second day's doubles match, the French team of Bolo Talotla and Le Runion defeated the English team of Lee and Hughes 6-3, 8-6, 6-2. The details of the match are supplemented below.

French Doubles Win over England 159

In the first set, Hughes served, and the French team attacked with all their might. In an instant, they took a 4-0 lead. The English team勉力fought back to win two games, making it 4-2, then 5-2, 5-3. The French team finally won the set 6-3.

The second set was more balanced. The English players were quite capable of handling the situation and often attacked the weakest, Brulunion. As a result, after 2-2, they took a 5-3 lead. At this time, Bolo Talotla became angry and quickly caught up, joining forces with Brulunion to launch an attack. They tied the score at 5-5 and once took a 6-5 lead. However, the English team tied the score again at 6-6. Bolo Talotla felt a sense of urgency and did not dare to be careless. He rallied and forced the English team to be cautious, changing from attack to defense. The French players finally won again 8-6.

At the beginning of the third set, there was overcast skies and rain seemed to be coming. The French team was eager to end the match, and their fierce attack left the English players at a loss. The French side first took a 2-0 lead, followed by 2-1, 3-1, and 4-2. Finally, they won 6-2. After two days, England still led 2-1.

Victory News of Nanyang Business School's Philippine Basketball Team 171

Defeats the Entire Philippines College of Economics Team - Forces Out the Entire Min Columbia Team

The Shanghai Nanyang High Commercial School's basketball team's Philippine campaign, in its premiere match in Min, defeated the College of Economics, this year's runner-up in the entire Philippines high school basketball tournament, 63 to 39. Following with 49 points to 30 points defeating the elite Columbia team who comprised the Min summer basketball tournament. There's a tendency for the team to be successful at the very start. The processes of the South Trading Business' consecutive crushing of strong enemies in the two battles is written down in brief in what follows.

Painful Strike of College of Economics 172

4PM on the dot, athletes from the two teams each stood in a basket making casting and passing practices. the physiques of the Philippine team were tall and strong, while the South Trading Business team were delicate. The onlookers thought of the Philippine team as last year's basketball runner-up for the Philippines College, with high skill, so worried for South Trading Business School who faced this strong team. The match was divided into 4 quarters, each quarter had 10 points. At 4:30 PM, Referee Yang Shufang called the team captains on both sides to choose a basket, and after the whistle blew, the war curtain was pulled. Wu Zibin from South Trading Business center forward, Chen Jinzhi received with the horizontal technique, and then it was passed to Zhou Cheng, and Zhou single-handedly charged straight in, taking advantage of the situation and casted. The ball rebounded, and before sighs from all around subsided, Wu Zibin captured the ball on the left, passed it far to Zhou Cheng who was hidden beneath the basket, and actually casted it in, therefore the record was opened. Wu Zibin continued to advance and casted another ball in, and the ratio was 4 points to 0 points. The Philippine team thought that South Trading Business' momentum was unusual, and vigorously tried to resist, casting a ball from a distance using its right forward, and followed South Trading Business with 2 points to 4 points. At the start of the contest, the two sides inevitable had excessive misgivings, and acted like something was forgotten from what was standard, particularly the South Trading Business School constantly revealed excessive eagerness, and there was no less than 4 instances when the ball was casted into the basket, but rebounded out. Fortunately, all the generals were able to calmly perform, and entered afterwards, and silently inspected the opponents' weaknesses, and taking advantage of the vulnerability to advance and attack, and actually Chen Jinzhi Zhou Cheng sequentially entered a ball, creating a ratio of 8 points to 2 points. Fighting to South Trading Business School with 10 points to 5 points in the lead, the Philippine team vigorously counter-attacked, and points gradually increased, and South Trading Business School refused to fall behind, and vigorously suppressed, and in the middle of the two sides' struggle, the points gradually drew closer, with the difference between scores often at one or two points of slightness. Until the first quarter was completely over, and the Philippine team was in the lead with a ratio of 15 points to 12 points. The 2nd quarter began, and South Trading Business School substituted Wu Zibin for Han Zhenyuan, and with this main general, the entire team suddenly seemed to be reborn with dragons and tigers, and using the East Strike West method, fought so that the Philippine team lost all their strength and flowers, Chen Jinzhi Han Zhenyuan Zhou Cheng connected attacks, and during this period, South Trading Business School's edge was greatly revealed, and with a ratio of 21 points to 6 points, stole back the position of leadership. Adding the first and second quarters together, South Trading Business School remotely led with 33 points to 19 points. In the 3rd quarter, the two sides easily swapped locations and continued to fight, and the South Trading Business school's athletes occupied the upper hand in the two above-mentioned quarters, and would not let the opportunity go. Cai Wen, the two guards, have already reinforced the defense, and moreover provided the front line with a supply, and the front line generals Chen Zhou had repeatedly obtained a carriage from the rear sending ammunition rations, and invaded enemy territory repeatedly to build work, repeatedly achieving miraculous feats. During this period, the opponent only had the work to resist, and did not have any power to counter-attack, and therefore South Trading Business School greatly won this quarter with 15 points to 5 points. In the last section of the match, Han Zhenyuan and Chen Jinzhi acted its fast-transfer fast dispatch technique, and built feats section by section, while the Philippine team had failure was already just under the eyebrows, and vigorously countered-attacked desperately, and although this section was tied with South Trading Business with 15 points to 15 points, but the points lost in the former three sections was too excessive, there truly was a sigh of having no choice but to more than make up for its loss. Therefore, when the match was over, the total result with 39 points to 63 points, suffered a miserable defeat to the South Trading Business.

Great Victory Over Columbia 173

Riding high on their previous victory, the Nan Shang team once again took to the field to face the Columbia Academy, an all-star team comprised of elite players from the Min Xia Ling Championship. The Columbia team was further bolstered by the addition of the Young Men's Association stars, Yang Dequan and Guo Pizhen, making their strength even more formidable. Having witnessed Nan Shang's decisive victory against a strong opponent that afternoon, local Chinese residents flocked to the evening game in even greater numbers than before. The game was originally scheduled to begin at 7:30 PM, but due to electrical repairs inside the venue, the lights were delayed until 8:20 PM. As the silver whistle of Yang Shufang sounded, the two teams began their pursuit of the ball, darting east and west. In a moment of intense back-and-forth action, Cai Yanxiong suddenly burst through the crowd, and with a flick of his wrist, the ball sailed into the basket. A thunderous cheer erupted from all around. With Cai having opened the scoring, Zhou Cheng then capitalized on a foul by Yang Dequan to score a free throw, bringing the score to 3-0. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the Philippine team urgently called a timeout to discuss strategy. After the game resumed, Yang Dequan managed to score a point from a free throw, breaking their duck and making it 1-3. From then on, the two sides were evenly matched, with the difference in score rarely exceeding one or two points. The score was tied no fewer than five times, from 9-9 to 13-13, then 16-16, and finally 18-18, until Han Zhenyuan scored a free throw to break the deadlock at 21-20. From that point on, the intensity of the game was breathtaking, and the audience's expressions of excitement as each team scored were almost frenzied. Wan Laolao Min of the Philippine team suddenly scored a basket, making it 22-21. Later, Chen Jinzhi and Han Zhenyuan of Nan Shang employed their lightning-fast shooting skills, scoring several consecutive baskets to take the lead again at 29-22. In the fourth quarter, the Nan Shang forwards unleashed a barrage of shots, shining brilliantly, and the score soared. Although the Philippine team frequently changed players and mounted a desperate last stand, the overall momentum had shifted, making it impossible to salvage the situation. Finally, as the whistle blew, the fierce battle came to an end, and the scoreboard displayed a final score of 47-30, with Nan Shang claiming another victory.

News

The Ministry of Education Recently Announced Four Curriculum Standards (1) 176

The Ministry of Education announced the following four high school and junior high school curriculum standards on the 28th:

(1) High School Geography 177

I. Objectives

(1) To enable students to understand the phenomena and relationships of natural and human geography in various regions of China and the world.

(2) To enable students to understand the Premier's industrial plans, national defense situation, and China's position in the world.

(3) To enable students to understand the position of various countries in the world and the current international situation formed by geographical relationships.

(4) To enable students to understand China's position and the international situation, so as to cultivate their awareness of loving and developing national interests.

II. Time Allocation

Taught over three academic years, two hours per week. The first, second, and third semesters focus on Chinese geography. The fourth and fifth semesters focus on foreign geography. The sixth semester focuses on physical geography.

III. Teaching Material Outline

(I) First, Second, and Third Semesters: Geography of China

(1) Regions

(3) Central Region

(3) Southeast Region

(4) Southwest Region

(5) Northeast Region

(6) Plateau

(Note) The above six regions should be described according to the scope of the Premier's industrial plan railway system.

(II) Key Points for Regional Description

(1) Transportation: (A) Land transportation: railways, highways, and existing provincial and county roads; (B) Water transportation: steamer routes, sailing routes, mileage and seasons; (C) Air transportation: air routes; (D) Telecommunications: wired, wireless, long-distance telephone, radio stations; (2) Cities, Ports, Harbors, and Port Construction; (3) Agriculture, Mining, Forestry, Animal Husbandry, Aquaculture, and Salt Production; (4) Industry and Commerce; (5) Residents, Population, Language, and Religion; (6) Topography, Climate, and Soil; (7) Water Conservancy (Surveying and Irrigation, including dike construction and dredging, etc.); (8) National Defense.

(III) The Relationship Between Chinese Geography and Economy

(1) General overview of China's population distribution and immigration issues; (2) General overview of Chinese farmers' cultivated land and land issues; (3) General overview of China's agricultural products and their statistics; (4) General overview of China's food supply and import and export statistics; (5) Types and statistics of China's important industrial products; (6) Statistics of China's recent import and export types and quantities; (7) The relationship between China's imports and exports and various countries; (8) Foreign economic power in China; (9) Changes in China's recent customs revenue and tariff system; (10) Distribution of China's mineral resources and developed and undeveloped mineral resources.

(II) Fourth and Fifth Semesters (Translated names temporarily adopt the person and place name table published by The Commercial Press)

(1) Asia

(1) Nanyang (Southeast Asia)

(A) Regions: Siam and the areas governed by Britain, France, America, the Netherlands, and Portugal; (B) Main products and cities; (C) General overview of the political situation and races in various regions; (D) The situation of overseas Chinese in various regions; (E) The influence of Singapore on transportation and military affairs in the Far East; (2) India: (A) Regions and major cities; (B) Nationalities and religions; (C) Economic and cultural situation; (D) The past and present of British rule in India and the general situation of the Indian national movement; (3) Iranian Plateau: (A) Regions: Persia, Afghanistan, Balochistan; (B) Main products and cities; (C) General overview of races and politics; (4) West Asia: (A) Regions: Turkey (focusing on the general situation of construction after its restoration), Iraq, Arabia, Syria, Palestine; (B) Main products and cities; (C) General overview of nationalities, religions, and politics in West Asia; (5) A general overview of the political divisions and nationalities of Central Asia and the Caucasus; (6) Siberia: (A) Topography and climate of Siberia; (B) Population and important special products of various regions; (C) Siberian Railway and important cities; (D) Nationalities and political system of Siberia; (E) The situation of overseas Chinese in various regions; (7) Japan: (A) Location, territory, and evolution; (B) Topography and climate; (C) Products, industry, and commerce; (D) Major cities; (E) Residents and population; (F) Education and culture; (G) Japan's external aggression and conquered territories: Ryukyu, Taiwan, Korea, Sakhalin, and trusteeships in the Pacific; (H) Japan's aggressive intentions towards the Asian continent and Nanyang; (I) Japan and the Pacific and its military preparations.

(II) Europe

(1) Soviet Russia: (A) The political organization and nationality overview of Soviet Russia; (B) Main products and cities; (C) Soviet Russia's economic policy; (D) Soviet Russia's military preparations; (E) Education and culture; (2) Baltic States: (A) Finland; (B) Estonia; (C) Latvia; (D) Lithuania; (3) Poland: (A) Population, transportation, and major cities; (B) Its rise and construction after the European War; (4) Germany: (A) Location and regions; (B) Industry and commerce and major cities; (C) Population, political, and cultural overview; (D) The general situation of Germany's reconstruction after the European War; (5) Scandinavia: (A) Denmark (focusing on its agriculture and rural life); (B) Sweden; (C) Norway, with a general overview of Iceland, Spitsbergen, and Greenland; (6) Netherlands (focusing on its water conservancy, industry, commerce, and colonies); (7) Belgium; (8) Great Britain: (A) Location and regions (England, Wales, and Scotland); (B) Industry and commerce and major cities; (C) Population, political, cultural, and military overview; (D) The economic and military relationship between Great Britain and its overseas possessions; (9) France: (A) Location; (B) Industry and commerce and major cities; (C) Population, political, cultural, and military overview; (D) France's overseas possessions; (10) Switzerland (focusing on its industry, commerce, and political organization); (11) Austria; (1)(2) Hungary; (13) Czechoslovakia; (14) Balkan Peninsula (Romania, Bulgaria, Greece, Yugoslavia); (15) Italy: (A) Location; (B) Industry and commerce and cities; (C) Population, political, cultural, and military overview; (16) Iberian Peninsula: (A) Spain; (B) Portugal.

(III) North America

(1) United States of America: (A) Location, territory, and evolution; (B) Topography and climate; (C) Products, industry, and commerce; (D) Major cities and transportation; (E) Population, political, and cultural overview; (F) Alaska, the Panama Canal Zone, Hawaii, and others; (G) The United States and the Pacific and its military preparations; (2) Canada: (A) Population, major products, and cities (4) South America

(1) Regions: Mexico, Central American countries, West Indies, South American countries, Argentina, Brazil, Chile.

(1) Independent countries in Africa (A) Egypt, Suez Canal; (B) Abyssinia; (C) Liberia; (2) The general situation of Africa under the rule of European powers.

(VI) Oceania

(1) Australia: (A) Regions; (B) Main products and cities; (C) Climate, population, and political overview; (D) Australia's development and the White Australia policy; (2) New Zealand; (3) Islands of Oceania.

(VII) Polar Exploration.

(III) Sixth Semester: Physical Geography

(1) The Earth's Movement and Shape: (1) The Earth's rotation, revolution, and changes in day and night and the four seasons; (2) The Earth's longitude, latitude, five zones, and orientation; (2) The Land Boundary: (1) The distribution of land and water; (2) The classification of landforms: mountains, plateaus, plains, basins, valleys, rivers, lakes, swamps; (3) Boundary: (1) Distribution of the ocean; (2) Ocean currents; (4) Air and Water Quantity; (5) The Biosphere: The relationship between the distribution of organisms and topography and climate.

IV. Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Assignment Requirements

(1) Enable students to use maps and statistical charts as a reference for learning; (2) Provide extracurricular self-study materials and books as reference materials for independent work; (3) Facilitate students' use of field trips and various observation practices for on-site observation; (4) Enable students to practice preliminary surveying and mapping to seek the correctness of geographical concepts; (5) Enable students to use comparison, statistics, and note-taking to seek the integration of learning content.

(2) Key Teaching Points

(1) Should be connected with junior high school teaching materials to improve the content level, avoid repetition, and give students a strong interest; (2) When teaching, use the textbook as an outline of the teaching materials, and provide students with guidance to collect reference materials as the basis for independent research; (3) When teaching, design methods should be used as much as possible to enable students to design independently; (4) When teaching, use photos, picture cards, specimens, models, slides, and experimental instruments as an aid to intuitive observation; (5) When explaining teaching materials, attention should be paid to whether there are omissions in the textbook or recent changes, and supplementary teaching materials should be added, and attention should be paid to actual life and current affairs related to China and foreign countries.

It is reported that the affirmative side of yesterday's topic was the advantages and disadvantages of resuming diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia versus severing diplomatic relations, and the advantages and disadvantages of early marriage versus late marriage, with Wu Baojin attending as a judge.

The Oldest Female Student in this City 179

Liu Xiuying, 53 years old, is the wife of a worker. She studies at the labor school of the wharf business office 丨 Her goal is to learn arithmetic to keep accounts for her husband 丨

The wharf business office in this city, in order to promote labor education, established three labor schools in April of this year. The first is located at the Pudong wharf on the opposite bank of Yangshupu, the second is located at the Dongchang wharf in Pudong, and the third is located on Changan Road in Zhabei. Each school currently has more than 40 students, and the first class will graduate next month. Among them, Liu Xiuying, a female student in the first school, is already 53 years old, from Jiangbei. She has white hair but is still energetic, and her teeth have not fallen out. Her husband, Huang Jianbiao, is 56 years old and works as a foreman on the wharf. He has three sons who are all wharf workers. Several members of the family are illiterate. Every day, the allocation of wages requires the help of others, which not only costs remuneration but also feels inconvenient. Therefore, the woman decided to enroll in the wharf worker school and asked the teacher to learn accounting and basic arithmetic for the purpose. The wharf business office authorities praised this greatly and gave her a book allowance and instructed the school to give her special treatment. This woman is actually the oldest female student in this city. Compared to the 65-year-old woman in a certain Huangpu school who was regarded by Westerners as the oldest primary school student, they can be called shining brightly one after the other.

A Bird's-Eye View of Shanghai's Medicine in the Last Decade (Continued) 186

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter Five: Administration of Medicine, Section Three: Recent Government Orders

I will now summarize the products of these deformed political views, which are the following five government orders suppressing new medicine: (According to my own experience since starting my practice, I have been subjected to one registration law from the Ministry of Internal Affairs of the Northern Government, one from the Health Bureau during the era of the Shanghai Bund Commissioner, and five from the National Government, for a total of seven times. Fortunately, I have always met the qualifications each time.)

A. The "Provisional Regulations for the Management of Physicians (Western Medicine) by the Shanghai Special Municipality Health Bureau of the National Government" in the 16th and 17th years [of the Republic].

B. The "Provisional Regulations for Physicians" promulgated by the Ministry of Health in the 18th year. The most difficult aspects of this were the issues of being directed by the police and the qualifications. After the Shanghai Medical Association requested leniency for the general practitioners outside the association, the Ministry of Health drafted a petition, but the Executive Yuan rejected it.

C. The "Western Medicine Regulations" promulgated by the National Government on May 7th of the 19th year. However, this regulation stated that the date of implementation would be determined by order. To this day, there has been no order, so it is unknown whether it is in effect or not.

D. The "Regulations for the Higher Examination for Western Medicine Physicians" promulgated by the Examination Yuan on December 27th of the 19th year. This regulation stated that it would be implemented on the day of promulgation, but there has been no examination to this day.

E. The "Measures for Variable Certification of Physicians" passed by the Legislative Yuan and promulgated by the Ministry of Interior (naturally drafted by the Department of Health) in the 21st year, which was the result of repeated petitions from the new medical community across the country.

The above government orders have been extensively researched by Dr. Wang Qizhang. He authored an article entitled "Several Doubts Regarding the Qualifications of New Physicians," which was published in the Double Tenth Special Issue of the 21st year and reprinted in the Medical Affairs Compilation, Issue 13. I will take the liberty of extracting a few key points from Dr. Wang's article, which will be sufficient to represent what I want to say, so as not to waste ink in this article. "Among these five public orders, either the later order is issued, and the former order becomes invalid; or the two orders coexist. Needless to say, there is the issue of their retention or abolition, but it is clear that the government authorities have no definite direction or consistent system for managing physicians in these four years."

"The Provisional Regulations for the Management of Physicians (Western Medicine) promulgated by the Health Bureau became invalid after the Provisional Regulations for Physicians of the Ministry of Health were promulgated, but in fact, they have not become invalid."

"What the National Government promulgated was the Western Medicine Regulations, and what the Ministry of Health promulgated was the Provisional Regulations for Physicians. Fortunately, to this day, the National Government has not ordered the date of implementation; otherwise, those who are called physicians would immediately have to be called Western medicine physicians."

"What the Examination Yuan promulgated was the Western Medicine Physician Examination Regulations. Since its promulgation to this day, no Chinese medical practitioners have taken the examination, and it can be said that no one is qualified to practice."

"The clumsy policy of cutting the feet to fit the shoes and restricting the qualifications of physicians is nothing more than a mockery of a few new physicians who have gone astray (referring to those who are not from schools or from unregistered schools?)."

"The current review and examination are all about cleaning up a few new physicians who have already been established, and there is no concrete method to stop unqualified physicians from being produced in the future and to supplement qualified physicians."

"Under one government, it is sometimes tight, sometimes loose; sometimes strict, sometimes laissez-faire, causing a group of people to have unreasonable thoughts and to obtain things by chance."

"Sometimes the municipal government allows him to practice, but the Ministry of Health does not allow him to do so. The feeling of one tightening and one loosening is really unpleasant."

"The variable certification method limits it to those who started practicing before the 18th year and have interned in a hospital for more than five years or graduated from a school for more than four years. Both can obtain certificates, but in society, what about those who do not meet the two qualifications but have already obtained certificates? Furthermore, what is the method to prove that they started practicing before the 18th year?"

Mr. Yu was indeed elected as the honorary president. After Mr. Huang passed away, Mr. Du Yuesheng was subsequently elected as the president, and I am now remotely leading the hospital affairs under the name of general manager and do not see patients.
